**Welcome to the Big & Dandy 2C-I Thread**


![299px-2C-I-Chemdraw.png](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fupload.wikimedia.org%2Fwikipedia%2Fcommons%2Fthumb%2Fc%2Fcd%2F2C-I-Chemdraw.png%2F299px-2C-I-Chemdraw.png&hash=0fd5e85440126cdbc1ee9f9ce3c75a55)

![f4lcud.jpg](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fi45.tinypic.com%2Ff4lcud.jpg&hash=69cc9355125afc0be082fa5bb9ae4bbb)

**Final 2C-I Question (Dosing it in water)**


The first time I did 2C-**B** it was thrown into water by my guy, stirred up, and I drank it. It was 20 MG to be exact. The trip was absolutely amazing and to this day stands as one of my favorite trips.


Now, I'm about to have 20 mg of 2C-**I** and I wanted to know if I can just take it and throw it into a shot glass of water, stir it up with a toothpick (or anything, really) and drink it. Then refill the glass about 3 more times to make sure I get everything.


Would this work perfectly fine **WITHOUT** ruining the potency of the 2C-I?


Also, please note that I don't have any alcohol (Vodka) to put it in and I'm not going to injest it.


Thank you in advance, Bluelighters. You guys help so much.

<!-- POST END: id=8894767 -->

That should be just fine. Many people prefer to place the compound in a small paper (rolling paper) and form a small pill that can be swallowed easily.

What I do for sublingual administration is crush up an Altoid, mix with 2C-I, and place under tongue and hold until it's completely dissolved.  Altoids cover up the 2C-I pretty well (not completely) and dose is stronger / comes on faster.


Or a capsule that you have supplements in could simply be emptied and the 2C-I put in there and swallowed.

100 mg 5-HTP capsules are be big enough to hold typical doses of the 2C compounds.


Whenever you want to take some just open the cap and pour the contents into a drink.


Later, when you want to take 2C-*, you can use the empty cap.


This works pretty well if you can't find caps or don't want to buy them for some reason.

I do exactly what you suggest.  I measure it in distilled water after weighing it, stir it in a shot glass and dose.  I've considered refilling it to make sure I get everything but I haven't attempted this yet.  My batch of 2c-i needed a lot more stirring than the 2c-e I got from a different vendor though.. I had to stir pretty seriously and it took maybe 10-15 mins to fully dissolve.

<!-- POST START: id=8896047 num=9 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2010-10-18T17:52:51+0100 -->
### Post #9

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|

| Page | 1 |

Hell, I just dump the 25-30mg of  straight powder on the back of my tongue and down with a little sweet drink of some kind.


For sublingual use (lets me use a little less... 15mg, 20 for a stronger trip), I first swish with a Listerine-style mouthwash, brand name or store generic, containing both alcohol AND MENTHOL, both of which increase absorption thru mouth tissues, for a minute, and dump the raw powder directly under my tongue... doesnt really taste too bad or burn more than a little.. adding a crushed small mint does sound like a good idea... actually I think mint might help it absorb as well.  After about 20minutes I will take a drink, swish and swallow to be sure it all get into my system in a timely manner just in case.  It seems to come up quicker under the tongue, but also not last quite as long, but still great.


Note these amounts lean toward the "strong" end of dosing.

<!-- POST START: id=8896852 num=13 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2010-10-18T21:31:47+0100 -->
### Post #13

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8896852 |
| Author | DwayneHoover |
| Author ID | 95165 |
| Date | Oct 18, 2010 at 9:31 PM |
| Page | 1 |

Sure, that'll be just fine.  DON'T take within 3 hours of a meal... this can greatly reduce strength and increase time to come on ALOT... a little something like a quickly absorbed protein drink is OK... add 2-3 grams of Vitamin C (use non-acidic Ester-C form) as well as other antioxidants you can afford... CO-Q10 and Alpha-Lipoic Acid are both good to prevent neural stress from free-radicals, they also protect the heart muscle and enhance body's oxygen and energy utilization.


DO NOT take with or within 30 minutes of anything very acidic like Orange or Grapefruit juice... some disagree but I find and pharmacological research all say that phenethylamine absorption is significantly slowed/blocked by added acids in the stomach like these, as well as first-pass elimination via kidneys is increased.  [notice that on a script bottle for ANY amphetamine, they now add a little sticker to this effect... if you dont believe me google for presescribing/dosing info from official med sites, or wikipedia]

<!-- POST END: id=8896852 -->

<!-- POST START: id=8898329 num=17 author=greenmeanies author_id=138956 date=2010-10-19T05:05:57+0100 -->
### Post #17

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8898329 |
| Author | greenmeanies |
| Author ID | 138956 |
| Date | Oct 19, 2010 at 5:05 AM |
| Page | 1 |

^ and as far as dosing, the most precise method will be liquid measurement.


If you have a milligram (0.001g) scale, then you will be able to dose 20mg (0.020g) accurately for a single dose.


If you have a centigram (0.01g) scale, then you CANNOT accurately dose a single 20mg (0.02g) dose. The scale is NOT PRECISE at this level and you MUST use liquid measurement.


See the big and dandy liquid measurement thread for more info, and don't hesitate to ask if you're confused about your scale or any calculations! we want to make sure you get a safe dose!


EDIT: i just saw your mention of blotter dosing. 20mg of 2C-I will not fit on a blotter. Drugs that will 'fit' on blotter must be active in the 1-2mg range, because any more than that will be visible as a white powder that will fall right off the paper instead of staying trapped in the fibers.

<!-- POST END: id=8898329 -->

|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8898356 |

| Page | 1 |

my experience has been, it lasts for years. I once got paranoid years ago and buried my stash, and 2ci was the only thing that survived months underground (although mainly due to the well-sealed bag). Last dose was taken a few months back, which made it... 4 years after purchase date, and the trip wasn't any different dosage wise than when first received.


I'd suspect storing it as powder would be better.


GuatamaToro, let us know how it goes/went and how it compares to your memories of the Brominated form. I personally think difference would only be in dosage, but I'm sure its been discussed and people have come up with all kinds of little special subjective differences. In my experience, the experiences weren't close enough to remember exactly, but it seemed the same (CI vs CB).

<!-- POST END: id=8898356 -->

**visuals**


/\ If you read his post or had a basic concept of dosage, you'd know that answer. /\                      

    Maybe you shouldn't be playing with chemicals, no offense?


Alright next topic...


2C-I visuals! vs 2C-E, 4-tryptamines and LSD.


I remember the first time I did 2C-I, one morning. 16mg. What lovely, "digital" visuals I had! This was my first PEA experience, but had done 4 different tryptamines. CI had more soft, bright and glowy ones... eh its hard to put into words. 


2C-E seemed to have darker visuals, or a dark impression to them anyway, mentally and emotionally. However, CE at a laser show was amazing, and both an old friend and I mistaspliff (he still here? don't know) both felt like we wanted to "melt into" the visuals shown on the planetarium. It was more intense, and I ended up having to drive :/ never again. A "yield up ahead" sign will NEVER look the same, and i still get kind of creeped out/giggly when I see one thanks to CE.


So far, 4-aco-dmt has been visually inferior to CI at roughly equal dosages, however, mentally the imagination is exponentially more enhanced on 4-dmt.

<!-- POST END: id=8898412 -->

## Page 2


<!-- POST START: id=8898529 num=21 author=greenmeanies author_id=138956 date=2010-10-19T06:09:44+0100 -->
### Post #21

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8898529 |
| Author | greenmeanies |
| Author ID | 138956 |
| Date | Oct 19, 2010 at 6:09 AM |
| Page | 2 |

I'm really sad to say that i didn't get enough experience with 2c-e to comment on its visuals. it was my first 2c-x and i was completely enamored with low dose (2mg rectal, or 4mg oral) ability to completely change the flavor of a day. slight color enhancement, incredible increase in the appreciation of music, and don't even get me started on the tactile sensations! but i gave away most of it so i never got a chance to try any dose higher than 16mg oral.


2c-i i've taken orally up to 24mg and it does have a very malleable visual quality at that level. Points of light (stars, headlights, lighters, etc) would sparkle like those fireworks that shimmer and crackle. Subtle fields on the other hand (clouds, grass, etc) would fuzz over with a 'smoky' appearance that continuously shifted brightness and shade.


as for closed-eye visuals, i was HEAVILY reminded of my own mushroom OEV/CEV experiences by the 24mg 2C-I closed-eye visuals. Heavily biased toward orange, yellow, with contrasting purple and green. All continuously warping and swirling. 2C-E on the other hand felt like a laser show in my eyes-- bright lines and patterns of thin color against a black background, with more of a 'strobe' effect and less swirly motion.


i hope that i will find 2c-e again in teh future, because i think i liked the body high of 2c-e better than that of 2c-i. it's kind of hard to tell without a direct comparison though.

<!-- POST END: id=8898529 -->

### Post #22

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8898571 |
| Author | Symmetrical Daze |
| Author ID | 39827 |
| Date | Oct 19, 2010 at 6:26 AM |
| Page | 2 |

2C-I is quite mild visually, for me. But it has had its moments... like when no trypts have been ingested for a long time. It shines more in positive mental effects.


My problem with 2C-I is concern for aftereffects. I used to get depression afterwards that was not as intense but similar to MDMA comedown. Of course, most amps do that. But I remember doing it frequently for a while, and not feeling right for some time. This is quite inspecific and subjective I know, but its true for me.


I admit to wanting to try it again though, its been a long time.


[I have my first trip on erowid](http://www.erowid.org/experiences/exp.php?ID=19017) ... i think under RetroGrade. i know it was like 8 years ago. I thought I had posted it here but turns out I don't think I had an account yet.


After reading my trip report, I realized this is the only time I actually vomited from 2C-I, but nausea was present nearly all the time on comeups (I've probably done this stuff 35+ times), but usually subsided near peak, but sometimes reignited at comedown. 


How is the nausea for you guys, and what is the timing for it like? Ever vomited?

<!-- POST END: id=8898571 -->

**The key to consuming 2c**


2c-i and 2c-e are insanely water soluble. Therefore mixing with water is better than just eating it like a pill.


but the best way to consume any 2c-i, 2c-e, 2c-b...


SNORT IT its WAYYYYYYYYY more intense

I always end up regretting eating it. Snorting it makes it hit you quicker and harder. the peak is way more intense than eating it. Stop being a bunch of POOOOOOOOOONS and just snort it!%)


as for visuals. 2c-i has more in your face hallucinations (things moving around and looking geometrical) as apposed to 2c-e

2c-e brightens and darkens things. more colors.


all the 2c visuals look like things are being brought in and out of focus


and as for my dosage. i normally snort 30mg+ of 2c-i or 2c-e anything less just wont cut it

and as for the nausea, SMOKE WEED the entire time and you will feel better/hallucinate more

after all weed is a psychedelic =P


acid owns 2c though. lsd is my favorite psychedelic because its not as crazy as 2c. you feel like you have more control over things. 


2c does whatever the hell it wants! lol


side note: on 2c-i i get this insane urge to make fun of/mess with things, people or ideas

in a very brutal way

<!-- POST START: id=8928132 num=32 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2010-10-28T06:04:31+0100 -->
### Post #32

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8928132 |
| Author | DwayneHoover |
| Author ID | 95165 |
| Date | Oct 28, 2010 at 6:04 AM |
| Page | 2 |

You ought to feel modestly stimmy from 15mg 2C-I, only some visuals a little over threashold, but nothing too impressive.  For some people it ends up being more than that, but IME this is the most common reaction to such a dose... you'll at least find it enjoyable and not a waste I bet.


25mg should have you seeing thick flickering trails behind anything that moves, and an extremely nearly cosmic Zen-like state where stopping all internal verbalizing and all other thought processes is second nature and you feel like your're blurring into the background.

<!-- POST END: id=8928132 -->

<!-- POST START: id=8929054 num=35 author=jeezits author_id=152821 date=2010-10-28T15:58:07+0100 -->
### Post #35

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8929054 |
| Author | jeezits |
| Author ID | 152821 |
| Date | Oct 28, 2010 at 3:58 PM |
| Page | 2 |

N3wt, why not just eat a few mgs or better yet 1mg (better yet a fraction of an mg) just to make sure it isn’t some other weird stuff?  You have 500mgs so that should give you plenty of room to play around and find a good dose right?  You say you are being paranoid but yours is a damn good situation in which to be paranoid.  The best advice is to start ridiculously small, at least for that first initial trial, and slowly work your way up.  I mean, look at some of these vendors these days and some of the drugs they are playing around with.  


My first 10mg dose of 2ci was a definite +++ experience, and now I’m pretty sure 10mg could never give me a +++. I’d need at least 15-16mg for that now.  The first time you take 15mgs will probably be the hardest you ever trip on that dose, which is another good reason to start low and work up.  You’ll keep some of the magic in the experience longer that way.  Good luck with your adventures.

<!-- POST END: id=8929054 -->

<!-- POST START: id=8929197 num=36 author=raui author_id=161233 date=2010-10-28T16:55:51+0100 -->
### Post #36

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8929197 |
| Author | raui |
| Author ID | 161233 |
| Date | Oct 28, 2010 at 4:55 PM |
| Page | 2 |

I started at 15 mg, it wasn't bad at all.  I actually noticed the visuals before the body load or any body high at all.  Took about an hour to kick in.  I was pretty stimmed but only speaking, it wasn't like I needed to pace around, I was fine just sitting at the comp during some of it.  And yes, text is definitely interesting.   It was a very euphoric experience with a lot of laughs.


My next experiment was going to be 20mg but my scale was iffy so I just erred on the side of caution and went for 18mg.  I'll probably go for 22mg next time.  My 18mg experience was a diff come up though, I noticed the body load about 30 mins in this time.  Was a bit more edgy, we had also come inside from a bright day into a dim house so I was getting flashing shades of red in my entire vision, which made my trip to the bathroom very intense, lots of morphing with the patterns on my tile floor.  I got this contrast on 2c-e too but it was more like a general film/layer of static light or darkness.

My gf and I spent a lot of time just looking for visual catalysts this trip, we'd turn the lamps on and check out the shadows on the wall morph around, we even noticed a lot of similar shades of color like our bedroom had a whole RBG spectrum.   Then we'd lay on the floor and stare at the shadows from the ceiling light, we have a very interesting fixture.


Still no trails or crazy patterns though.  Even though the visuals were about on par with my research of 2c-e(10, 15 and 18 mg), the 2c-e showed a bit more patterns morphing around, especially staring at my skin.  Both are pretty good for vivid visuals though, skin in general is very interesting, I was very entertained by my girlfriends freckles.

I'm still looking for some crazy colorful kaleidoscopic patterns like I got with amt, ordered some of that recently and hoping to appreciate it like I did years ago.  It seems the 2c-x substances I tried are mostly just visual when it comes to morphing and shadows/light but I still need to research them further.  And don't get me wrong, I'm not just looking for visuals here.. I'm under playing how intense these experiences were emotionally and mentally but that's a bit harder to discuss all the meaning I was able to find in everything.  As far as an emotional comparison, I'll say I cried a lot more from my 2c-e trips.  I did get very emotional the day after my last 2c-i trip though... damn Toy Story 3 and Bill Hicks documentary.

<!-- POST END: id=8929197 -->

I get some definite visuals from 12mgs, tons of visuals from 15mgs, and even tons more visuals from 18mgs which is the highest I’ve gone because the physical stimulation of 2ci while tripping can wreak havoc on my headspace, especially when combining with cannabis which is a must for me every time.  However, after reading so many reports I realize I’m relatively sensitive to the effects. 


I don’t think 2ci is nearly as psychedelic on the mind as 2ce or lsd, but I do get tons of open and closed eye visuals from it. Nevertheless, I do find 2ci to be fairly psychedelic on the mind, especially mixed with cannabis, just not as much as other things.

<!-- POST START: id=8931550 num=38 author=n3wt author_id=169106 date=2010-10-29T05:25:22+0100 -->
### Post #38

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8931550 |
| Author | n3wt |
| Author ID | 169106 |
| Date | Oct 29, 2010 at 5:25 AM |
| Page | 2 |

I ended up trying out 10mg to start.  I didn't get any nausea or body load to speak of at that dose, felt mildly stimulated, like I'd had some coffee.  Visuals at that level were actually more than I expected, though very user friendly.  I only got a bit of a startle when my Jim Morrison poster which I'd been watching slowly morph suddenly morphed very quickly.


I tried taking another 8mg to up the experience, but I was around 4 hours in by that time so all it really did was prolong the experience.  Between around t+6 and t+6:30 it did amp up a bit though, the most intense visual being watching my ceiling spinning opposite to my fan in muted purples and yellows as pixels sort of rained down.  I only got this if I really let my eyes relax though.


All in all a fairly successful experiment.  I'm not feeling any after effects at all really, other than being a bit tired.

<!-- POST END: id=8931550 -->

<!-- POST START: id=8974268 num=39 author=n3wt author_id=169106 date=2010-11-11T03:22:47+0000 -->
### Post #39

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8974268 |
| Author | n3wt |
| Author ID | 169106 |
| Date | Nov 11, 2010 at 3:22 AM |
| Page | 2 |

So I thought I'd update this with my further experiments.


I've gone as high as 24mg in the time since, and I've had some interesting experiences.  As the dosage increases visuals get more intense, and music euphoria goes through the roof...the only problem is the stims really start to get in the way of having a good time.  I'm not a big fan of stimulants period, so the massive amount of stimulation that comes from a 20mg+ dose is really uncomfortable to me.  I find myself constantly having to stop myself from grinding my teeth, and constantly moving around, very restless.


I guess I always find myself reaching for more psychedelic effects and less stimulation.  That said, it is an interesting substance.

<!-- POST END: id=8974268 -->

<!-- POST START: id=8982470 num=45 author=n3o author_id=168060 date=2010-11-13T08:58:23+0000 -->
### Post #45

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 8982470 |
| Author | n3o |
| Author ID | 168060 |
| Date | Nov 13, 2010 at 8:58 AM |
| Page | 3 |

I'd like to report success with dissolving 2C-I in alcohol.


I dissolved my usual dose, about 30 mg - (it seems high, but for some reason I always need more than everyone else to get the same effects) - in some alcohol. I then drank it on a mostly empty stomach (4-5 hours after lunch).


The visual effects this time were at least twice as strong, and music euphoria was fantastic. Huge trails, and everything seemed kind of shiny and glittery. When I laid down on the bed and closed my eyes, I saw what I guess could be described as LSD-type visuals (alas, I can not compare from direct experience). I was giddy and happy the entire time - much better than anything I can get from methylone.


I think the alcohol improved absorption - significantly. I've had 40 mg before in plain water and still never got anywhere close to 30 mg dissolved in alcohol. I don't believe the alcohol affected the trip - it was not even one drink's worth.


I should also add that I supplemented with 5-HTP, but I don't think it affected the trip in a huge way, as I've supplemented before.


Just ordered some more 2C-I - definitely my favourite now.

<!-- POST END: id=8982470 -->

| Field | Value |

I consider 2C-I to be barely psychedelic.  For me, it was like the buzz of MDA with far more visuals, stronger (and longer) stimulation, and almost none of the emotional or mental effects.  It did make me laugh a lot at times... and like someone else said, it gives a wicked rush combined with nitrous... and yeah for a few minutes while I chased 3 carts with 3 more carts and then 3 more carts, I realized how my energy was just a tiny drop of water in a huge ocean or something...  but that's about it for depth on this one!  Speaking of gasses, it also made me feel like I had intestinal gas or something at higher doses, but I don't think I ever actually did.  All in all, it's great for sex.  Otherwise...  I never seemed to get much from it.  I would get bored, take it, and then ask myself "oh God, why did I take this shit again."  Oh yeah, brutal hangovers... though maybe not as bad as MDA!  I don't think anything leaves me feeling as fried as MDA....  but I love it anyway.

<!-- POST END: id=9099263 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9116463 num=53 author=Bi0hazardOpeth author_id=165416 date=2010-12-17T16:02:32+0000 -->
### Post #53

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9116463 |
| Author | Bi0hazardOpeth |
| Author ID | 165416 |
| Date | Dec 17, 2010 at 4:02 PM |
| Page | 3 |

I also wanted to point out, that those who are considering snorting 2c-i, that you should be cautious beyond just the painful burn it creates. 


Snorting 2c substances increases the potency of the dose substantially and creates possibilities for potential health issues given the strong dose that hits all at once. Many times people will reduce their oral dose by half or 1/3 before snorting it.


Just saying, Be Careful...

<!-- POST END: id=9116463 -->

> 			100 mg 5-HTP capsules are be big enough to hold typical doses of the 2C compounds.
> 
> 
> 
> Whenever you want to take some just open the cap and pour the contents into a drink.
> 
> 
> 
> Later, when you want to take 2C-*, you can use the empty cap.
> 
> 
> 
> This works pretty well if you can't find caps or don't want to buy them for some reason.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — n3o said:


Wanted to follow up on this. Recently I traveled and wanted to bring a single dose of 2C-I.


I took one 5-HTP capsule and removed half the contents, added a dose of 2C-I, and then added back as much 5-HTP as I could before closing up the capsule. I then put the capsule back into the full bottle of 5-HTP pills.


It's a good combination since I like to pre-load with 5-HTP anyway - and I don't have to arbitrarily waste an entire 5-HTP pill just to hold the small bit of 2C-I.

Hahaha the title of this thread reminded me of my ridiculous friend who took ~43mg at a renegade last summer, with no prior psychedelic experience (except rolling). 


He bought two caps off me (I weighed out a bunch between 20-23mg a piece) and took one at sunset. I swear I told him to only take one, that two would be a super intense experience probably unfit for our environment, and that it takes a fair while to come on. Well this kid got impatient and decided to take the second one 2 hours in because he wasn't feeling it enough. He spent a good chunk of the night standing away from the group staring at the moon, mouth agape.


Apparently he had a good time! Said he wouldn't be doing that kind of dose for a while though..


Anyway, another thumbs up here for 2c-i. One of my first, and still one of my favorite rc's.

2C-I was one of the first RC's I fell for.  This was years ago, but I would space my doses by the work-week and always have a great Friday night.  I waited for my roommate/girlfriend to go to sleep and I'd eat some of it and the stimulation would keep me up until sunrise.  I'd watch it from my balcony as it came up between the mountains.  Sometimes there would be a lingering visual overlay which made everything look like it was a puzzle that had been put together without missing pieces.


Anyway, just reminiscing.  2C-I is one of my favorites even though I haven't taken it in quite a while.  I've got a little on the way, so it will be nice having that around for a special night when I'm not looking to trip out as hard as I might on some other chemicals.


Really looking forward to taking some of this stuff with methoxetamine.  ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

I've heard some whispers, but anyone know anything substantial about mixing 4-ac0-DMT and 2c-i ?

They're both "fun" psychedelics, (less deep than others but still deep) and i think they would synergize nicely. Think about it:

~4-aco is a relatively strong tryptamine that is rather sedating

~2c-i is a relatively strong phenlyethlamine that is rather stimulating

~both have relatively the same dosage (so maybe take 2/3 or 1/2 of both?)


The perfect sedated/stimulated inverse trip combo?

Any thoughts or experiences???

<!-- POST START: id=9207366 num=65 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-01-11T21:55:51+0000 -->

> [Psyke said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9207334)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Any thoughts or experiences???
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Psyke said:

On NYE I had some experience with a 4-AcO-DMT/LSD combo (~20 mg + ~100 mics) and this can definitely fuck up your plans...

Since I have a lot of experience with 2C-I, I'll try to extrapolate.


Definitely tone your 4-AcO-DMT dose down a notch extra compared with your 2C-I.

I suggest you take 80% of your normal 2C-I dose and somewhere round 50% of a typical 4-AcO-DMT dose.

Perhaps better to drop the 2C-I sometime before the 4-AcO-DMT, so you can zone in easily and don't end up in some super-enhanced sick bodyload nightmare.


For myself, I would prolly start with 32 mg of 2C-C, since I find this ultimately relaxing.

After about 90 mins, I would drop a capsule containing 14 mg 2C-I and some 14-16 mg of 4-AcO-DMT.

Perhaps drop the 4-AcO-DMT a tad later, I usually decide such things *on the spot*. ;-P

<!-- POST END: id=9207366 -->

I just did this combo last week actually, 16mg 2C-I and 18mg 4-aco-dmt.  They didn't seem to get on top of each other too much, it was more like they were working side by side.  By that I mean it wasn't terribly intense, it was just the effects of being on a middling dose of each at the same time.  


It was alright, but I wouldn't say there is really any magic to be had by combining the two.


I dosed the 4aco about an hour and a half after the 2C-I, seemed to work out pretty good.

i did a bunch of 4-aco-dmt whilst coming down from 2c-i.  i haven't ever done 4-aco-dmt on its own.  the resulting 4-aco trip was pretty insane... and by insane i mean approaching psychosis.  granted, i dosed the 4-aco at like midnight or 1am, and late night tripping often gets me close to psychosis.


physically it felt fine though.  watch your dosages.  i took like 50mg of 4-aco thinking that there would be cross-tolerance between it and the 2c-i i had taken about 4 or 5 hours beforehand.  looking back i am not sure if that was sound logic.

<!-- POST START: id=9214983 num=69 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-01-13T19:01:43+0000 -->
### Post #69

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9214983 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Jan 13, 2011 at 7:01 PM |
| Page | 4 |

> [Psyke said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9214853)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I'm pretty sure tryptamines mainly work with your seratonin, and phens mainly work with your dopamine receptors so...
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Psyke said:

You should definitely double check your pharmacology source mate. ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

Unless you mean amphetamines - which are also phenethylamines - phenethylamines exert most of their effects through the 5-HT2A and 5-HT2C receptors (which are serotonin receptors).

Beside that, tryptamines don't work with serotonin, they mimic serotonin and bind to serotonin receptors.

If this is what you meant I apologize for nitpicking, but you shouldn't think in terms of serotonin depletion when using tryptamines. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=9214983 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9214998 num=70 author=helium-4 author_id=70722 date=2011-01-13T19:05:23+0000 -->
### Post #70

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9214998 |
| Author | helium-4 |
| Author ID | 70722 |
| Date | Jan 13, 2011 at 7:05 PM |
| Page | 4 |

I find there to be a very noticeable cross tolerance between phenethylamines (2c-i and 2c-e, my experiences) and tryptamines, though I will say that there isn't as much of a cross tolerance as I've seen with LSD and tryptamines.  


I say as a rule of thumb majority of your traditional psychedelics will have some cross tolerance with each other due to agonism of the same serotonin receptors, like the 5ht-2a.

<!-- POST END: id=9214998 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9228289 num=71 author=Psyke author_id=172840 date=2011-01-16T21:48:20+0000 -->
### Post #71

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9228289 |
| Author | Psyke |
| Author ID | 172840 |
| Date | Jan 16, 2011 at 9:48 PM |
| Page | 4 |

Deos anyone notice the visuals from 2c-i are different than almost any other hallucinogen?

I get no visuals from it, it seems, and then i focus on a certain area; i.e. wooden floorboards and end up getting some of the most intense visual displays of my life. For me you have to concentrate for them to appear, and if you decide you're not gonna have any visuals anymore, then they disperse. I noticed i was receiving mescaline-ish visuals over 12 hours after i took a 25mg dose.


Also, after reading/researching around, i figured this chem was going to be more on the "light" side of things compared to lsd/psilocin.


Boy was i wrong. Probably 10x the introspection that lsd has for me, with 50x the visuals.

There appears to be no ego-loss but more so.... ego expansion?  


I also experienced Synesthesia like nobody's business.

<!-- POST END: id=9228289 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9230753 num=79 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-01-17T12:04:54+0000 -->
### Post #79

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9230753 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Jan 17, 2011 at 12:04 PM |
| Page | 4 |

> [DwayneHoover said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9230701)
> 
> 
> 
> 			what dose of 2ci did you use, in what timing/sequence relative to lsd?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — DwayneHoover said:

I have tried the 2C-I/LSD combination for at least ten times.

Most of the time at big festivals, so my dosage might have been a bit on the safe side.

My suggestion is you take about 20% off of your normal 2C-I dosage (that would translate 15-16 mg in my case).

Dose LSD just as you would normally do, though I wouldn't pass the 200 mics mark on the first try.


I generally chose between two dosing regimens:

- Drop 2C-I and LSD together in a capsule, with my blotter cut into very small pieces

- Eat LSD first and drop a capsule with 2C-I about 2 hours later

Both options were nice, with higher dosages of LSD I guess the second one is preferable.

<!-- POST END: id=9230753 -->

guys could someone tell me if 2C-I stored in a powerade bottle in a vodka solution in the fridge would be OK after a few months? it may have not been air tight for some time, and the fridge is quite cold. i am concerned about the fact it was not air tight - will this cause any degradation? thanks

<!-- POST END: id=9240965 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9241008 num=84 author=allium author_id=143046 date=2011-01-19T22:09:16+0000 -->
### Post #84

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241008 |
| Author | allium |
| Author ID | 143046 |
| Date | Jan 19, 2011 at 10:09 PM |
| Page | 5 |

I stored my 2C-I as 10mg/1ml solution in tap water at room temperature(but in dark) for more than a year, and it don't seem that it lost it any potency. 

Don't worry, 2Cs(in particular 2C-I) are stable compounds when stored in solution. Some alcohol(AFAIR ~17% or more)will prevent bacteria growth, so it is good idea to add it.

Also, personally I wouldn't advise using powerade bottle, because it is made from plastic. I am no chemist and I don't know if alcohol can absorb plastic. But common sense tells me that if there are no high-alcohol drinks sold in plastic bottles, then there may be certain reasons for it.

<!-- POST END: id=9241008 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9241046 num=86 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-01-19T22:20:31+0000 -->
### Post #86

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241046 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Jan 19, 2011 at 10:20 PM |
| Page | 5 |

Chemicals in solution usually don't degrade because of exposure to air.

Even if, your container was probably *almost* airtight, and your fridge would be like minus 20 degrees?

Temperature is the real bitch when it comes to degrading, so I think your 2C-I will be just fine! ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


Alcohol can't absorb most plastics BTW.

Only some of the more high-end plastics used in laboratories etc. can dissolve in alcohol.

However, it *can* absorb certain nasty compounds to make the plastic malleable, like bisphenol A.

But plastic bottles that contain drinks usually don't have much of these substances.


BTW, alcoholic beverages are definitely sold in plastic bottles.

Also, in our laboratory we use 'absolute' alcohol (which is 99.9% anhydrous alcohol); this comes in plastic bottles.

And this kind of alcohol has to be absolutely pure, because it can really fuck up your experiment if not (plus they charge like € 170 per 1L bottle...insanity!).

<!-- POST END: id=9241046 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9241276 num=94 author=Psyke author_id=172840 date=2011-01-19T23:25:57+0000 -->
### Post #94

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241276 |
| Author | Psyke |
| Author ID | 172840 |
| Date | Jan 19, 2011 at 11:25 PM |
| Page | 5 |

*changes topic*


> The thyroid gland helps to regulate many key body functions, including the production and release of human growth hormone (HGH), Vitamin K production and regulation (Vitamin K regulates how much oxygen that blood platelets can carry), production and regulation of epinephrine (adrenaline), and to a lesser (but seemingly just as important) extent, the regulation of the mood regulating chemicals serotonin, norepinephrine, and dopamine. 
> 
> 
> 
> 2. 2C-I is a iodinated chemical structurally related to epinephrine, norepinephrine, and dopamine. 
> 
> 
> 
> 3. Iodine is the heaviest halogen available (there is one heavier, Astatine, but it is a rare, radioactive, and completely unusable atom in pharmacology). 
> 
> 
> 
> 4. Iodine has NEVER been used in any psychotropic (mood-altering) chemicals other than thyroid medications. 
> 
> 
> 
> While many of Shulgin's chemicals employed halogens (ie. 2C-C, 2C-B, 2C-F, 2C-T-21, and also their amphetamine homologues), all of them, with the exception of 2C-I and its amphetamine homologue DOI, employ the lighter, and consequently 'friendlier' halogens fluorine, chlorine, and bromine. Even in medical pharmacology, iodine is never used outside thyroid treatments. For example Wellbutrin (bupropion) uses chlorine, and Prozac (fluoxetine) uses fluorine. 
> 
> 
> 
> 5. 2C-I has a high affinity for serotonin HT2-type receptors, and to a lesser extent norepinephrine and dopamine receptors, all of which control critical aspects in regulating mood. 
> 
> 
> 
> Even without testing or any kind of clinical evidence, one could conclude that by introducing a chemical into the body that has a high affinity for mood-regulating receptors, contains a halogen that not only is much heavier that anything that normally enters said receptors, but also is used in the regulation of an important endocrine gland, there is going to be trouble. 
> 
> 
> 
> Who knows what kind of long-term damage 2C-I may have on people, not only those with thyroid problems, but healthy individuals as well!? Until some clinical data exists that shows 2C-I as not being neurotoxic, I would recommend that you stay away from taking this chemical.
> 		
> Click to expand...


^this is from an erowid health risks experience report.

What do you guys think?  2C-I and DOI really are the only drugs that employ iodine, besides certian thyroid medications.


Is this good evidence that it indeed does cause thyriod problems?

It'd be quite a shame if it did. Full report: [http://www.erowid.org/experiences/exp.php?ID=39567](http://www.erowid.org/experiences/exp.php?ID=39567)

<!-- POST END: id=9241276 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9241476 num=99 author=mesial author_id=165594 date=2011-01-20T00:31:09+0000 -->
### Post #99

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241476 |
| Author | mesial |
| Author ID | 165594 |
| Date | Jan 20, 2011 at 12:31 AM |
| Page | 5 |

Just tried 2C-I for the first time this past weekend so I thought I would share a bit of my experience here in the big and dandy thread.  My dosage was 18mg (after a test of 4mg a few nights prior which did have an effect, although slight). I did take 25mg of diphenhydramine in order to reduce body load.  


My previous psychedelic experiences include mushrooms (up to 3.5g cubensis) so its really all I can compare it to.  Within 60mins I began to get some visual alerts, patterning of the floor and walls.  This is somewhat like the patterning I get from mushrooms but just a bit different.  

The visuals progressed to halos around every reflection of light that would cast a rainbow type prism look throughout my home.  The visualizer on the TV looked like it was extending past the television.  I found myself staring at a painting on my wall of a long road lined with trees that have shed their leaves.  They were waving back and forth and morphing all over the place.  A shower with candles and hot steam made for some interesting visuals as well.  I took my 18mg orally at 2:30PM and was able to fall asleep by 10:30pm.


Outside of this, I didn't find myself really gaining much from the experience.  As some previously stated in this thread, at many points I would be stuck not really thinking of anything, just staring off and wondering "why am I doing this?"  Very neutral experience for me.  I would feel an urge to do something, then I wouldn't want to do it like 5 seconds later.  My wife and I went for a walk in a park next to where we live and it just wasn't as profound as I was hoping.  I felt zero euphoria during this trip.  Mostly neutral outside of a few chuckles here and there.


I did break out some nitrous and enjoyed smoking some cannabis and taking nitrous while getting lost in my visualizer with music.  Every light in the room would sparkle and give off a prism type look, almost like the varying colors you see when light shines on oil or soap atop of water.  


Mushrooms are deeper mentally for me, without a doubt.  And although I find myself working through my mind on shrooms, it is almost always followed by immense euphoria as I come to certain conclusions about myself and life in general.  


I am a big guy, did I dose too little? I didn't want to push it for my first time.  Another interesting bit of information is that I am still experiencing the floating patterning you see when you let your eyes relax.  It is dissapating as the days go on but it is somewhat bothersome since I've never had this happen to me following a mushroom experience.  When I smoke cannabis, the patterning is ramped up even more.  I wouldn't call it HPPD because its only been two days and it certainly is not affecting my daily life.  Not sure if I'm going to try this one again?

<!-- POST END: id=9241476 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=9241503 num=100 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2011-01-20T00:53:09+0000 -->
### Post #100

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241503 |
| Author | DwayneHoover |
| Author ID | 95165 |
| Date | Jan 20, 2011 at 12:53 AM |
| Page | 5 |

Your intense visual experience is unusual for only 18mg (for a big guy at that).   When I added diphenhydramine to 2C-E to lower bodyload my impression was that it also increased visuals.  This is the first know report of using it with 2C-I so, interesting... it would be nice to have people very familiar with 2C-I to try this combo and report (OK, I volunteer... when I get more... all out now).


FYI, I am pretty big (6'1". 200#), and find a notable increase in euphoria and visuals at 25mg.  Even at 20, effects are there but mostly in the body.  But when I hit 25 it just seems to blossom... brilliant colors, huge long tracers, buddha-like bliss.  But yes, it is quite emotionally neutral, and very clearheaded... NO headfuck, so if all sorts of intense bizzaro hallucinations is what you are looking for, 2C-I is the wrong drug.

<!-- POST END: id=9241503 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9241655 num=107 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2011-01-20T01:55:17+0000 -->
### Post #107

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241655 |
| Author | DwayneHoover |
| Author ID | 95165 |
| Date | Jan 20, 2011 at 1:55 AM |
| Page | 6 |

Oh yea, the DPH was really unnecessary with the 2C-I and I would suggest when you do it again to skip the DPH.  Perhaps that is what made it feel so "flat" for you.  2C-I really has no body-load except for stimulation, but that is part of what makes it work.  


2C-E is ALOT different.  It can cause intense nausea, and widespread very weird overall body aches and pains that can be REALLY uncomfortable for most people.  2C-I does *NONE* of this.  Anyway these are why to do DPH with 2C-E.  It's unnecessary with 2C-I and might alter the trip more than you want.


I would say wait ONE week, then try 25mg on an EMPTY stomach (no fruit juice or other acidic beverages like soft drinks [look for citric acid on the label], ingested acids lower the potency of all phenethylamines) with no DPH.  THATs how to tell what 2C-I is really all about.  If you ever smoke weed... have some of that available to accentuate the trip and perhaps smooth over any temporarily excess stimmyness.  But if you DO feel "stimmy", don't sweat it... its how you know the drug us working.  Ever done MDMA?  There is a period of stimmyness the first hour or so... (with 2C-I about 1.5 hours)... which then melts away to reveal the drug's psychedelic effects like the drawing of a curtain.  A beer with its hops and alcohol is also fine and would also be good for the stimmyness.


Unless you are like me and find a mental way to ENJOY the stimulation, like an exciting carnival ride... just try to relax and breathe deep and enjoy the "liftoff" like you are in the "Booster" phase of taking off in a space rocket.  Dont psyche-out and start to panic.... it will melt away soon enough, just ride it out and you will be rewarded.  If you panic and start to freak like some people, well then all bets are off.  A good way to take your mind off it is to watch some exciting or trippy movie that you can let yourself be absorbed into, smoke a joint, etc... you'll be fine based on your report above.  Good luck!!


Heres a graphic they used to play at peak intense psychedelic moments of Grateful Dead shows, spelling out NAMASTE in Sanskrit... try to stare at it for a whilefull-screen in a dark room when peaking, haha!


![NAMASTE-5-1.gif](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=http%3A%2F%2Fi268.photobucket.com%2Falbums%2Fjj20%2Fbunnyhoover%2FNAMASTE-5-1.gif&hash=86681d18128cfb25a232888f68382faa)

I have done MDMA, so I know the stimulation you speak of quite intimately ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  I don't mind it actually... I end up using the energy to dance, glove light, or talk.  I've had intense nausea from mushrooms but I noticed it was extremely psychosomatic, the more I would let myself go, the nausea would subside.  In fact, the reason I chose 2C-I first was because of how many people related the euphoria to MDMA.  


Well, I'm convinced to try this again.  Without DPH ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png) I think I was drinking soda on the come-up this weekend but I hadn't eaten in 2 or 3 hours.  I'll stick to water during the come up.  Is it okay to drink some juice mid-trip?  I always love fruit juice and fresh fruit while tripping.

<!-- POST START: id=9241767 num=109 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2011-01-20T02:35:26+0000 -->
### Post #109

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9241767 |
| Author | DwayneHoover |
| Author ID | 95165 |
| Date | Jan 20, 2011 at 2:35 AM |
| Page | 6 |

Sure, juice after its absorbed its not an issue and very good for you for the nutrients and the extra energy from the sugars etc. 


But I don't think Ive seen many reports that relate 2C-I to the euphoria of MDMA.  MDMA is very very... PERSONAL.   It makes you feel totally romantically in love with every single individual molecule.  Whereas 2C-I is very NOT this.  It kind of makes me feel like The Buddha of the Universe... somewhat remote and aloof, but still feeling a certain god-like euphoria at being able to feel the amazingness of it all, but on a much more mental, far far less emotional way than MDMA.

<!-- POST END: id=9241767 -->

> 
> Click to expand...
> — Psyke said:


that experience report has been discussed here before.  the person in question was taking medication for pre-existing hyperthyroidism.  i'm fairly sure that their unique reaction was due to the combination of the medication and the 2c-i.


enough people have used 2c-i without problems that i feel that it must be reasonably safe to use.


however, i do notice that 2c-i feels more difficult to renally excrete than other 2cs.  perhaps that is psychosomatic though.


someone else mentioned DOI--keep in mind that DOI is active at one tenth of the mass that 2C-I is active at.  this means that DOI is theoretically 10x safer for our thyroid glands than 2C-I is.

<!-- POST END: id=9241802 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9242255 num=114 author=IamMe90 author_id=176120 date=2011-01-20T04:48:05+0000 -->
### Post #114

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9242255 |
| Author | IamMe90 |
| Author ID | 176120 |
| Date | Jan 20, 2011 at 4:48 AM |
| Page | 6 |

that's exactly how it feels like to me, too. mescaline is euphoric for a psychedelic, but 2c-i is very dumbed down from it - the visuals feel less organic, as well.


however, when you dose high and with more intense ROAs (i've IM'd and insufflated before), it does get more of its own character - more bizarre of a headspace, things can honestly get a little dark - but interesting. my first time taking it (~25mg snorted) was actually more intense than my 2ce experience (although I have a feeling this could change if I dose higher on the 2ce), the visuals were insane, and I actually had an out of body experience where I heard myself talking on the phone from an observer's point of view. I was inebriated to the point where a family guy spoof of star wars was the most engrossing storyline I've witnessed. haha


people CAN make 2ci a powerful substance, but it requires high doses, intense ROAs, and *significantly* heightens the nausea and bodyload. and it certainly isn't like LSD or MDMA - very mescaline like visuals with a dark tinge.

<!-- POST END: id=9242255 -->

> Click to expand...
> — Psyke said:


It's a good combination actually, I always preload 2C-I with some 5-HTP now (one 100 mg cap). Just make sure to drink a cup or two of water when taking the 5-HTP - nausea hits if you take it on an empty stomach. One time I tried to take additional 5-HTP to extend the trip and it just ruined the rest of the trip due to nausea. Better to just let the trip run it's natural course.


Compared to trips without 5-HTP I would say that it adds more to the entactogen qualities.

<!-- POST START: id=9376947 num=130 author=greenmeanies author_id=138956 date=2011-02-24T04:16:00+0000 -->
### Post #130

| Post ID | 9376947 |
| Author | greenmeanies |
| Author ID | 138956 |
| Date | Feb 24, 2011 at 4:16 AM |
| Page | 7 |

i would consider that an idiosyncratic response.


Typical timeline for 2C-I for me is (iirc)

0:00 oral dosing, 16-22mg

1:30 come-up

3:00 peaking

5:00 plateauing

8:00 coming down

the rest is just residual stimulation

greetings shishigami, i know you saw my report on that other forum but just for the record,


A close friend 'apparently" tripped for ~36 hours, and didn't sleep for 50,

but i play that off as him being naive, large dose, and also being quite the dramatic fellow.


However, From personal experience I have had 14-16 hour trips off this stuff for sure. 

(30mg, so its a pretty high dose.)


EDIT; I would say the peak for me was around 9 hours in with gradually building intensity before that. Guess i'm alone on that

Hey so this is probably the worst idea ever but im going to ask anyways, if i did a super low dose of 2c-i could i get away with it being around ppl who dont approve of drug use? would a 5-10mg dose even be worth doing? im going to a concert and figure it will be pretty boring if im not on something ( i dont like the band). I can probably get away with telling them that i just took some xanax or something and thats why im acting weird they probably wouldnt question that. i have done a lot of other stuff and can keep my cool pretty well around people who dont know im tripping i just havent tried 2c-i before

<!-- POST START: id=9390267 num=133 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-02-28T20:43:17+0000 -->
### Post #133

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9390267 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Feb 28, 2011 at 8:43 PM |
| Page | 7 |

In my opinion, anything below 12 mg you can easily get away with without being noticed. When tripping, it isn't uncommon for me to get some groceries on as much as 18-20 mg, and even then I walk around the store quite comfortably. So if you take about 10 mgs there won't be any problem with those 'unapproving people'.


However, you could question yourself why bother going to a concert that is boring, resorting to drug use to entertain yourself. It's not something you should make a habit of IMO, catch my drift? ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=9390267 -->

^^ I wouldn't say that full stomach considerably slows absorbtion of 2Cs. I am almost 100% sure that psychedelic nausea related to activation of (5-HT) receptors in the brain; it is not normal nausea/stomach irritation, it is a "hallucination"(however, if you vomit - you vomit in reality![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)) 


I you have little experience with 2Cs, I would suggest having very light meal before the trip, so your stomach won't be full, but won't be absolutely empty.

<!-- POST END: id=9398123 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=9398239 num=155 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-03-02T22:22:47+0000 -->
### Post #155

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9398239 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Mar 2, 2011 at 10:22 PM |
| Page | 8 |

> [allium said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9398123)
> 
> 
> 
> 			I am almost 100% sure that psychedelic nausea related to activation of (5-HT) receptors in the brain; it is not normal nausea/stomach irritation, it is a "hallucination"
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — allium said:

It is quite likely that the majority of nausea experienced with psychedelics is related to 5-HT receptor activation. But this does not mean the nausea is a hallucination. Probably the highest density of 5-HT receptors can be found in the intestines, where they control motility. Activation of these receptors by a psychedelic would cause spasms in your intestines, leading to a nauseous feeling. Beside that, the chemoreceptor trigger zone (the area of your brain that controls vomiting) also contains 5-HT receptors. Since this area is more easily accessed than deeper parts of the brain (it's function is to puke out harmful shit, so makes sense it is relatively easy accessible), it is quite common for the nausea to come up before the experience is at it's peak.


Empty stomach means it is more likely for psychedelics to end up in your intestines, which can cause major discomfort. Therefore, an empty stomach is not advisable. A light meal about an hour before intake is usually perfect. You can also try and talk yourself through the nausea; realize it is only caused by activation of receptors and not because you are actually sick or ate something nasty. Once your trip reaches full intensity, the nausea usually fades out. Oh yeah, and puking won't really help in most cases, since the chemoreceptor trigger zone is still activated by the psychedelic in your blood i.e. brain.

<!-- POST END: id=9398239 -->

---

^ Really interesting, thanks for the explaination. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


> But this does not mean the nausea is a hallucination

>

<!-- POST START: id=9399855 num=157 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-03-03T07:26:16+0000 -->
### Post #157

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9399855 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Mar 3, 2011 at 7:26 AM |
| Page | 8 |

> [allium said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9398335)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Well, the feeling of nausea is real in the same sens in which seeing visuals is real, however visuals are considered hallucinations, so why nausea isn't? 
> 
> Anyhow, I wasn't sure if it is possible to call nausea "hallucination", that's why I quoted it. It is very different from usual stomach discomfort, stomach ache, and usual nausea. Of course, YMMV.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — allium said:

Well, first of all, technically speaking, visuals are not hallucinations but pseudohallucinations. But that's more about semantics than anything else, so fuck it... But in light of this debate/discussion/whateveryawannacallit, it does make sense to come up with this argument. Visuals are a pseudohallucination, in that the user can easily distinguish them from what is real; you can't interact with visuals in a serious way. However, the nausea is (in the majority of cases) directly caused by activation of receptors in the gut or in the chemoreceptor trigger zone (CTZ). Therefore, it is indistinguishable from 'real' nausea, since that is also caused inside the gut or the CTZ. So the nausea could be regarded as a true hallucination, since it is indistinguishable from 'real' nausea. But since it is not a product of the mind, I think the term 'hallucination' is out of place here...


Vomiting might provide relief yes, but it is generally not a healthy thing to do. Also, you can easily trick yourself in some placebo-effect of having to vomit every time instead of just blocking out the nausea until it takes off on it's own. This is especially well-known (at least where I'm from) in the case of MDMA, where some users are absolutely convinced they have to puke almost every time to start up their roll. In my experience, people that know how the nausea originates are usually a lot less likely to experience it, and that fighting the nausea mentally (i.e. waiting it out and just think of something else) creates a sort of natural resistance to developing nausea in your next trip. That's why I prefer to elucidate the mechanism and telling people to just wait until the dope hits the mind, instead of going puking. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=9399855 -->

gained lots of insights and was quite giggly, honest and humourous; mild empathy effects, but wasn't able to up the dose into any sort of visual effects due to the excess stimulation effects


perhaps it was the batch or my biochemistry (probably this) or the setting, but there was a good middle of the trip after i dosed a little more and it became rather uncomfortable, but drew calm in thinking through topics of spirituality. later it became quite euphoric and more trip like


perhaps with the 2c-b i will be trying soon i will stagger it with smaller doses at a time


worthwhile, but a bit uncomfortable

it made my spidey senses tingle

<!-- POST START: id=9503600 num=160 author=DwayneHoover author_id=95165 date=2011-04-03T03:33:11+0100 -->
### Post #160

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9503600 |
| Author | DwayneHoover |

> [3rd_I_blind said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9398239)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Empty stomach means it is more likely for psychedelics to end up in your intestines, which can cause major discomfort.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — 3rd_I_blind said:


HUH?  Were you high during basic biology class in grade school?   Stomach primarily DIGESTS substances (but some minor absorption occurs here, though not much); intestines ABSORB nutrients/chems into the bloodstream.


So, any drug has really got to make it past stomach into the intestine to work... except for LSD which is active in such minute amounts that it IS absorbed across mucus membranes enough to start working immediately.


But a drug like 2C-I that needs 15-25mg to work, has pretty much got to make it to the intestine to be absorbed and function... therefore slowing down this process by having it mix with food in the stomach is counterproductive.  You want the normally fairly rapid absorption of taking it with liquid on an empty or mostly empty stomach... a small snack is probably not going to affect it much, and may promote enzymes that make it absorb a little better possibly and if you are prone to nausea could help.


Personally I am not and have never once gotten nausea from 2C chems... friends who did it empty got off as expected within the hour...  those who did it after a meal complained that they were not getting off, or only felt "a little something" 2-3 HOURS after consuming.

<!-- POST END: id=9503600 -->

A couple weeks ago I took 18mgs of 2c-I, after a heavy lunch and heavy dinner. I waited almost 3 hours to take it, then I swallowed it in capsule form. I still felt very full, and there was still food digesting in my stomach. I didn't feel anything until 3hours later. It was like somebody hit a switch, and I was tripping hard. There was absolutely, no stomach discomfort. It was the most intense 2c-I trip i've had in the range of 15-25mgs. It may delay the effect, but it didn't effect the intensity for me.


Edit: Just for the record, I normally take 2c-x, 2-3 hours after a light meal, and it usually takes 45mins-1hour to kick in.

> 		
> Click to expand...
> — DwayneHoover said:

Ever heard of pharmacology and ADME? I might have been high during basic biology class, but at least I'm not using my elementary school knowledge in a discussion on this level... Uptake of any chemical is only dependent on physicochemical properties of the chemical and the part of the body where it is present, and thus can happen almost anywhere in the body. Since 2C-I is a primary amine, I suspect (know) it has a basic pKa and thus will primarily be taken up in the first part of the intestines.


However, theory is not always what will happen 'in practice'. I was just referring to personal experience with different 2C-chemicals, where me and my friends have observed that the abdominal nausea is much less when taken about 1 hour after a **light** meal. I believe a (partial) explanation is that activation of serotonergic receptors in the intestines creates excessive motility, leading to discomfort (and possible diarrhea). But this is probably a bit above your level, judging by the reasoning in your previous post. So perhaps you should do some reading on the matter first this time, before commenting on my mental clarity during kindergarten...

<!-- POST START: id=9512226 num=168 author=3rd_I_blind author_id=178736 date=2011-04-05T17:26:29+0100 -->
### Post #168

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9512226 |
| Author | 3rd_I_blind |
| Author ID | 178736 |
| Date | Apr 5, 2011 at 5:26 PM |
| Page | 9 |

> [killermunchies said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=9512089)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Compared to other stuff I've tried, the dosage curve seems much less linear.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — killermunchies said:

Technically, a dose-response curve is never linear both always sigmoidal in shape. The perceived difference in potency between two doses of the same substance is determined by the steepness of the curve and the percentage of 'response' that is physiologically (or psychologically, in this case) signifcant. As you might understand, a substance that is only noticable effective at 30% response will have a (perceived) linear dose-response relationship, since most substances are on the linear part of the curve between 30%-70% response. If your substance is already active at the 5% response level, doubling your dose can give a larger boost in response, since you are on the exponential part of the curve.


However, since we are talking psychedelics here, the dose is not the only thing that determines the intensity of the effects. There is also set, setting, your own body chemistry and some random factors. When also taking into account factors that influence pharmaceutical and biological availability (stomach contents, pH of stomach and intestines, blablabla), it becomes clear it's very hard to make any statements on the dose-response curve of a substance based on a few experiences. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=9512226 -->

With various 2C's i've heard of people reporting different amount of pain from different ROA's.  


I've heard some say 2C-D is not painful rectally, however I can say for certain that it IS painful if you squird it up yer butt..Same goes for 2C-T-7.


And the one time I did snort 5 mgs of 2C-D, it felt **quite** caustic, and I immediately regretted it.  That was after I read on Bluelight that "snorting 2C-D isn't that bad".   I know you're talking about sublingual 2C-I here, but...just sayin...So just because one person says it isn't going to hurt you on an internet forum, doesn't mean it's going to be the same for you.  Not trying to discredit what you said Dwayne, just trying to emphasize that YMMV.  Your mouth's mucous membranes are probably a lot tougher than the recesses of your sinus cavity too, so there is always that...


Remember, snorting any 2C-X drug is suppose to be quite painful, so there is at least some reason to beleive that holding a pure 2C-X drug under your tongue might give you some problems.  Trust me it's not THAT fun tripping with a lingering chemical burn that won't go away *glares at DPT*.....

I think the 2Cs must somehow activate the vanniloid receptor as they're fairly similar in structure (the vanilloid receptor is the one that makes chillies burn like buggery) to the aromatic part.


One thought is you could always try eating a little something with chillies in first before snorting it in the hope that the receptors will already be occupied with capsacin (then again that's hardly an improvement for most people!)


Oh and one way to avoid unpleasantness (well relatively) with DPT is, as Sherlock Holmes proclaims at the end of Hound of the Baskervilles,"Watson, the needle" (aLTHOUGH HE WAS A COKE FIEND). aLSO MUCH MORE ECONOMICAL WITH THE DRUG AND MUCH LESS UNPLESANT IF STERILE PROCEEDURE IS FOLLOWED


Fuck capslock horror!!

since we're on the subject of snorting 2c's...


anyone consider 2c-i extremely unique in its insufflation pain as compared to the other 2c's? 


snorting the other 2c's produced a big punch in the face that lasted for about half a minute... pretty much the same as snorting any other painful chem. 


but 2c-i was way more... "sinister." snorting it produced no immediate pain for a couple of minutes... and then suddenly an intense stinging manifested itself in my nose that lasted about 5 minutes, the drip about 30. my friend and I got this effect consistently while snorting it (about 6 times each for us) and it was far worse than any other insufflation experience we've ever experienced. *shudders at the memories*

<!-- POST START: id=9529765 num=189 author=MachoSavage author_id=183794 date=2011-04-10T23:51:58+0100 -->
### Post #189

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9529765 |
| Author | MachoSavage |
| Author ID | 183794 |
| Date | Apr 10, 2011 at 11:51 PM |
| Page | 10 |

Tried 20 mg of this last night, which was my first experience with PEA hallucinogens (not counting MDMA/M1). The powder didn't want to dissolve in room temperature vodka, but warming it up and stirring for a couple minutes did the trick.


Main effects were enjoyable without being overwhelming; I felt pretty much in control. I could easily get lost in my own thoughts if I let it happen, but there were none of the pushy racing thoughts I've felt with mushrooms. Tactile sensations were enhanced in a way that's hard to describe, and even imaginary touches felt quite vivid. (I was unable to persuade my gf to make sexy time, but maybe someday...)


Side effects were mild. Some body tension and aches but no nausea or anorexia. Often felt warm and sweaty, especially for the first couple hours. Tylenol seemed to help.


Pot greatly intensified the trip, especially the visuals. My gf noticed the same thing with K2 Blue, which reportedly led to her first "real" experience of a psychedelic thought process - she's taken 4-AcO-DIPT several times, but I think her SSRI detracts from the effects.

<!-- POST END: id=9529765 -->

<!-- POST START: id=9539307 num=190 author=fastandbulbous author_id=59655 date=2011-04-13T17:34:19+0100 -->
### Post #190

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9539307 |
| Author | fastandbulbous |
| Author ID | 59655 |
| Date | Apr 13, 2011 at 5:34 PM |
| Page | 10 |

As a rule, I've found that the phenethylamine psychedelics are much more subject to control as to how 'deep' things get ie it's much easier to return to concensus reality if needs be. Tryptamines are subject top less control and more of a case of just having to let go and go with the drug, rather than try and control thought processes. Then there's LSD, which for me has always been a case of 'hang on and hope for the best' as it's so in your face that any attempts to control the initial phases of intoxication (generally the first 3-4 hours) generally lead to rather unpleasant experiences. Another differfence I've found is that PEAs are much more outgoing and benefit from the input of others whereas tryptamines are much more of an internal experience, where it's a lot more common to close eyes and not really interact with people (DMT/DPT being the ultimate example where the best part of the experience is spent eyes closed, lost in an internal world even if others are present).


2C-I was, I found, one of the psychedelics that were the easiest to exert control over, the only one that comes to mind that was even moreso was 2C-T-21.


Of course al of the above observations are sependant upon the dose used - if you do things like shove 50mg of 2C-E up your backside, all aspects of being able to control the depth of intoxication are just swept aside because it's so intense an experience (and therefore not really recommended for most people). I once accidentally IMed 25mg of 2C-I (thinking it was ketamine in the vial) and then discovered that even a drug that normally wasn't too hard to deal with when used orally, can become a real white knuckle ride

<!-- POST END: id=9539307 -->

I see this thread is a bit stagnant, so I hope I can get my questions answered!


I'm a rather experienced tripper, I've done LSD in various doses over 25 times, shrooms about 15 times, 2C-B (not sure of dosage), DXM, and Salvia. I'm looking into picking up some 2C-I for an upcoming festival for me an my friends and was looking on some information on it, or some validation to my information.


-How long does 2C-I last on average when taken orally?

-What's the time frame range like, time for come-up, plateau/peak, and coming down?

-What's a good dosage on average?

-How does it feel in comparison to other psychedelics?


Here's what I've come to understand, please correct any misinformation. I've heard it takes up to two hours when taken orally for it to kick in. I've heard that it will plateau for roughly 2-6 hours, dependent on dose and then start to slowly taper off for another 2-4 hours, totaling about 6-10 hours total, with the later half being very mild. Erowid reports 10-25mg as a common dose, which seems a wide window. From reading around here many users say they've enjoyed 20mg, for someone who's experienced in tripping would this be a nice "easy"/fun trip? I've heard that overall 2C-I is mild and a great beginners psychedelic.


Any more feedback on this?

<!-- POST START: id=9823959 num=196 author=greenmeanies author_id=138956 date=2011-07-13T17:24:19+0100 -->
### Post #196

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 9823959 |
| Author | greenmeanies |
| Author ID | 138956 |
| Date | Jul 13, 2011 at 5:24 PM |
| Page | 10 |

Your information is basically correct.


Remember that with any drug, higher doses seem to kick in faster. I'd bet 100mg oral 2C-I will be a rocket ride to Neptune within the first hour. But yes, in general there is a full two hours of absolutely nothing before the trip actually takes shape.


As you have a bit of trip experience, I'd say you're fairly safe with anywhere in the 20-25mg range for a moderate +++ ride (Shulgin scale, not shroomery). Many people highly enjoy this compound in the 8-12mg range for a nice ++ time. I've even heard good things from people who only eat 3mg and get just a little mood lift.


As always with any new substance in your possession, use <1mg as an allergy test before eating half the bag. And use a scale please! ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


I will also repeat the benefits of "gradual" or "stepped" dosing, which can alleviate certain come-up tensions that are common to the 2C-family. Personally I have found 4mg oral at T+0h, followed by 18mg oral at T+1h, produces a much smoother trip than a single 22mg dose would. The same can be said for simply dissolving your full dose in a drink and sipping over the course of an hour. Seems the body has a better time adapting to the transition.


Some people call 2C-I a "toy" or "candy psychedelic", but it can be every bit as powerful as mushrooms or LSD in the hands of someone who wants to take it deeper. A friend of mine faced his inner demons and resolved to change his life on a 22mg 2C-I trip in the mountains. I was with him at the time on a similar dose, and I was just rolling on the ground laughing at the clouds while he was wrestling a bear in his mind o.o

<!-- POST END: id=9823959 -->

| Page | 11 |

**2C-I Phosphate**


Dr. Jekyl had a couple grams of 2C-I laying around so he converted it to the monobasic phosphate yesterday. Let it dry out overnight. Today Jekyl took 20 mg orally mixed with water. He commented that the taste was much less objectionable than that of the HCL. With the HCL you can never get the taste out of your head, with the phosphate it's not even a problem, Jekyl said. Very little body load. Very slight muscle tremors for a short time, not even unpleasant, Jekyl reported. He said nausea was virtually non-existent, though appetite was reduced. He did eat some though and it sat well in Jekyl's belly. 20 mg was a nice recreational dose, very controllable but with pleasant light visuals. When Jekyl smoked some hash it brought out the visuals nicely. Dr. Jekyl's conclusion was that 2C-I phosphate is vastly preferable to the HCL and at 20 mg a quite nice experience overall. Never will Jekyl use the HCL form again, he maintained. No human being should ever have to taste that s*** again, especially him, he pointed out emphatically.

<!-- POST END: id=10084073 -->

**2ci & comedowns..**


Im not sure if its the right thread to be writing on about 2ci,  i took it

people told me it was the same as 2cb but it was alot more intence and diffrent. 

i took about 10micrograms, wich isent alot as others i know have consumed, but still got a really intense 

come up. at first i didnt really know what was happening to me, i was upstairs in my room chilling out, when istarted feeling weird, like i couldnt catch up with my breathing!  i wasnt tripping out at this point. i came down stairs, thought id switch on the pc and try and figure out more about this drug.  all i saw was  ' lasts up to about 8 hours'  blablabla.. i was like woah reading this would probley deff me out more! :') so i switched that off, and put some music on, wich made me feel even more weird.  (obviously my body wasnt agreeing much to this comeup).   after 2 hours of feeling like dying. i felt ok but still having the odd feeling of probley becoming a cripple or something. i just chilled myself out and tryed to enjoy it as much as i could in the end i did end up enjoying it more. it was pretty crazy actually.  but i probley wouldnt take 2ci again. 


Comedown? 

i took the 2ci 2 days ago.

but today i am feeling some kinda weird. 

feeling in my body, i cant explain it much but it keeps feeling weird to breathe, really really light rushes, and tingles, and warm fuzzy feelings.. and my mind feeling too relaxed at random times..

would this be classed as a comedown? 

because some of these feelings is how i felt when i had 2ci. but it was MORE intense on 2ci. alot more.

or could it be anxiety? i dont usely get anxiety like this if it is. 

ive tryed googling' 2ci comedowns, and not found alot onit. 

but im also a everyday weed smoker 

and i havent had that for 2 days either!

so im compleatly confused. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)


help would be nice ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png) xx

cannabis is intensified for a day or two after a strong trip especially with the 2c's. So you get high and sort of slip into that 2c-i headspace. Don't worry it goes away quickly. It could be many things but there's a possibility for you.


i'm also assuming you meant milligrams, even at 10mg 2c-i is very weak, so I'm not sure. Was the dose measured properly with an accurate scale? it sounds like you had a pretty heavy come up, i don't get those with 2c-i until at least 30mg, maybe you took a higher dose than you think?

With no tolerance, 10mg of 2C-I can be very intense. The purity varies. 12mg of the best product I've run across had my wife hallucinating and full-blown tripping, borderline to overwhelming. I got it last summer from a good source and I've never felt the need to go beyond 18mg.


Your symptoms 2 days later however are likely just coincidental. I've never had a residual effect from 2C-I.

The next two days after 2c-i, if I rubbed my legs or feet against my bed or sheets, there would be this tingly euphoric sensation. A little hollow in feeling, but I remember doing it for a couple minutes at a time - because it was an interesting after-effect. I didn't really get anything like that while I was on 2c-i.


One other thing, I don't know how many other people experienced this. But I get a tingling sensations/very minor pains  in my teeth (usually front my front rows) that starts on the comedown. It's generally gone the same day - by the time It's fully dropped out of my system.

This'll likely be merged with the Big & Dandy 2C-I Thread, but since you're new you have a chance to reply first - and this might be left here a little longer first since this is quite a specific question that might get skipped over there.


What you're experiencing actually sounds like some left over vasoconstriction to me, some stimulants and stimulant psychedelics like the 2Cs cause this for certain people - I had it a bit with 2C-E.


It could also be psychosomatic, you often have slightly heightened senses for a few days to a week after taking psychedelics, so you might just be noticing things that were already there that little bit more ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=10235753 -->

which really disappoints me i like the 2c's and doc a lot more than i ever liked lsd i didnt get such a mental head fuck off 2c-i or doc like i did from L i found with 2c's and dox compounds your able to talk sense in yourself easier because of the stimulant effects 2c's and dox compounds always make me feel like a mild candy flip in low-average does and they can cause a lot of people to wig out and get over dehydrated and the long duration seems to be a factor in that with stimulation


trippin for 12+ hours is murder on your body and brain(atleast til you sleep,eat,drink ,etc)


also what was your ROA? nasal? oral? boof?


capsule?(ive seen weird cases where a capsule can not fully dissolve and leaves ya a present for later when you dont want it haha)


EDIT: extended 2c-i use is known for its hppd(Hallucinogen persisting perception disorder ) i felt an after glow for about 2 months after killing a gram of killer 2c-i in about 4-5 days

I don't know about that Dwayne. With the tolerance you build, it's easy to escalate doses pretty quickly. At a festival this summer, I took my first dose of psychedelics on the Friday morning, and after dtripping for all of Friday and Saturday, on Sunday morning a 50mg dose of 2C-C did absolutely nothing, nor did a drop of acid. I can definitely believe that someone could polish of a gram of 2C-I in a few days if they set their mind to it.
