**High dose 2C-I**


Tonight I've been reading a bunch of the trip reports for 2C-I on Erowid. Nearly all of them had dosages of 25mg or less, while there were a few about accidental overdoses of 100mg or more. I haven't been able to find anything in, say, the 30-60mg range. Are there any of you out there who have (intentionally ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)) done 30mg or more of 2C-I? I did 36mg once several years ago, and I'd like to visit that space again someday, but the body load was pretty tough (waaaay too much muscle tension).

<!-- POST END: id=10342023 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10345203 num=235 author=zn13bt author_id=160808 date=2012-02-19T15:38:14+0000 -->
### Post #235

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10345203 |
| Author | zn13bt |
| Author ID | 160808 |

| Page | 12 |

> [Never Knows Best said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=10344874)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Merged this since discussion that goes against HR needn't be emphasized by having its own thread, let's keep it low profile in the B&Ds.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Never Knows Best said:


Yeah, I was really hoping for reports in the 30-50mg range or so, not a bunch of bragging about surviving massive overdoses. Thought I made that clear, but I guess not...


I usually do 2C-I in the range of 15-20mg, and it's interesting enough but it feels a little superficial sometimes. A few times I've gone up to 25mg, and gotten a glimmer of a deeper headspace there, but the body load was verging on the uncomfortable. The one time I went higher than 25mg was when I tried it at 36mg, and in the middle of the trip I had a very profound experience of entity contact where there were these aliens standing around me in a semicircle communicating with me telepathically. What's really weird is that several years later, I was flipping through the book "Advanced Magical Arts" by R. J. Stewart, and in the middle of the book I came across a drawing (figure 11 in chapter 5, "Experience of the Underworld") which looked very much like the aliens I saw during that trip. I coulda plotzed. :D


Anyways, I think 2C-I has the potential to be a deeper psychedelic than most people give it credit for, and I was just trying to see if there was anyone else out there who has explored it at higher levels, and what they found there. The body load does get to be a problem at higher doses...36mg had me writhing around on my bed with my teeth chattering like crazy and my eyeballs wiggling so much that I couldn't see anything. Haven't had a lot of time for experiments lately, but maybe somewhere between 25 and 36 will turn out to be my sweet spot...

<!-- POST END: id=10345203 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10360018 num=237 author=omicamushroom author_id=148080 date=2012-02-24T21:18:34+0000 -->
### Post #237

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10360018 |
| Author | omicamushroom |
| Author ID | 148080 |
| Date | Feb 24, 2012 at 9:18 PM |
| Page | 12 |

Hello all,


I ate some 2cI the other day. Dose was about 15-16mg. I figured I would write up a pseudo-report and post it here rather than TR.


Backstory: I had stayed up very late the night before. When I lay down to fall asleep I was extremely drained, but was also hungry. I had no food though, and didn't feel like trying to go out and get some food. So I lay there. And I wanted to smoke some weed, but I was too drained to get up and load the bowl. I never actually slept though. I just lay there tossing and turning all night long. And then it was day time, and the girl got me up and we were on doing things around the house, cleaning and throwing things out. We had to move some things in the truck today, go to the dump and whatever else. I bought a bagel from d&d, but it sucked and I didn't really eat it. After some errands we went out to eat. I didn't eat though. I just drank booze and beer. We stayed there for more than 3 hours... so much for errands. We completed the errands, delivering some furniture to my place. When we got there and set everything up I was buzzing hard from the booze and mentioned, lets eat some 2cI. The girls had things to do, but they said sure. Within minutes I had the doses weighed up and we consumed them.... Probably not the best idea... but it was done and said.


The trip: Now, I hadn't really eaten anything today. My stomach was empty except for coffee milk and booze. ugh... Now the 2cI was beginning to take hold 30-40 minutes later. My stomach was not feeling it though. Neither was my girl. Our other friend (it was her first time with a 2c) had no body discomfort although felt weird during the come-up. I didn't expect much of a trip from the dose... I think mostly cause I was drunk, ad haven't had a strong psychedelic experience in a while... they've all been very light trips. For some reason the 2cI took complete hold 1.5 hours after dosing. I was tripping good. It was very acid like. 

The visuals surprised me very much. Our friend was working on some artwork, and so I tried my best to help. I was playing with her supplies and paper. I looked at a blank sheet of white paper, and my mind was blown away by the patterns in the paper. Our friend was having trouble drawing because the lines on the paper were wiggling too much. We were all tripping strongly. It was good, but somewhat unexpected. 

We talked a lot about the ups and downs of life. We had a funny moment where we each exclaimed that we had been feeling like shit the past couple days. And we all agreed, but then we tried to set a date to when we started feeling like shit.... and we said shit, maybe its been our whole life. We laughed at how absurd this was. All our conversations were changing scope... being inside the box to outside the box, so to speak - talking about the now to talking about the whole. I felt extremely detached from the world, not in a ketamine way, but in a psychedelic way. 

I was blasted, and was in +3 territory. We all loved it. Me and my girl, for some reason, had a lot of stomach discomfort... It wasn't terrible, but we had to keep puking out of our butts. I think this was on account of our diets that day and the previous day.. and the booze. I walked to the store at one point, and being in the store felt so odd. Walking through the park felt odd... but all in a good way... I was seeing life unfold. I was more aware of everything outside my purpose (my purpose being to get food). Normally I would walk and see nothing, but now I looked at the outlines of the trees, and the space between all these things. Memories flooded me of all my prior walks. 


Come down: The actual trip lasted 4-6 hours... I wasn't really keeping track of time. We all came down to a certain level and were left with some stimulation. I didn't sleep for another few hours. I waited until sunrise to go get some sandwiches and milk, so that I could eat and get my diet back to healthy, considering the past couple days I was pretty bad to my diet. 


Conclusion: 2cI is really awesome. It is very acid-like in my opinion. I liked where my mind went. The visuals were impressive. I feel like they work better when you keep the dose smaller, for some reason. I think I hit too much of a mind-fuck to see the visuals when I get to higher doses. This has been the same with 2ce. With 2ce I'll eat 12mg, and get loads of visuals, but if I eat 25mg I'm given a complete mind-fuck, and I don't really realize the visuals. I have eaten 2cI at higher doses also... 25-30mg or so... and was not as aware of the visuals as I was in this trip. I think it could have also been due to the strangeness of the situation... It's hard to determine. 


My advice. 15-18mg of 2cI is awesome. 


P.S. this hasn't been proofread, and it took me only 5 or so minutes to write up. Sorry if my writing sucks, and if it is hard to follow. I think that my main conclusion has something to do with being surprised at how 16mg of powder put me out of this world for a little while. It was pretty euphoric. 


P.P.S I have not eaten 2cI in close to a year.

<!-- POST END: id=10360018 -->

| Field | Value |

> [zn13bt said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=10342023)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Tonight I've been reading a bunch of the trip reports for 2C-I on Erowid. Nearly all of them had dosages of 25mg or less, while there were a few about accidental overdoses of 100mg or more. I haven't been able to find anything in, say, the 30-60mg range. Are there any of you out there who have (intentionally ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)) done 30mg or more of 2C-I? I did 36mg once several years ago, and I'd like to visit that space again someday, but the body load was pretty tough (waaaay too much muscle tension).
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — zn13bt said:


As well as quite a lot of 10-25mg doses, I've taken 30mg, 35mg, 40mg and 60-65mg. I've also had roughly 70mg of 2C-E, unintentionally.


Experiences are interesting. I had more problems with the body load around the 30mg range than with higher doses - I was a bit too scattered to focus on any physical discomfort. Coordination goes out the window - on 40mg it took me 15 minutes to get up two flights of carpeted stairs (they were flowing downwards like water, most disconcerting) and on 60-65mg I'm pretty sure I spent the peak lying naked on my bed rubbing myself up and down with my hands. At 40mg it also took me about 5 minutes to figure out that the discomfort I was feeling was thirst, and another 5 minutes to figure out that I could fix it by filling my glass with water... which is why I started to try to climb the stairs! Visuals remain completely grounded in reality at 40mg and apart from a couple of hours at the peak, the same at the highest doses I've taken... what I mean is, you can tell what everything around you is, including recognising people. Headspace is generally positive, but gets increasingly disjointed and unfocused as dosage rises - I've never had any particularly profound or mystical experiences with the stuff, nor any intense epiphanies or realisations, but on the flip side I've never had any bad experiences and have only ever had two bouts of unhappiness or paranoia that were easily dealt with. I find it a fun, light-hearted, comparatively social psychedelic at lower doses and an interesting but ultimately unfulfilling one at higher doses - the experiences are all fun, but they don't make it beyond that and you lose a lot of coherence, attentiveness and memory of the experience.


50mg is probably the highest I'd recommend (inferring from the two doses around it) if you're interested in high-dose 2C-I, experienced with the stuff and build up to that level over a few well-spaced trips. I can't imagine it being remotely unsafe and I had no side-effects that were even slightly worrying. Duration seems to increase at higher doses - detectable effects after about 12 hours at the highest two doses, about 10 hours at 40mg, etc. Factor that in to your preparations if you do try it. 


My favourite dose is 15mg or so. Low enough to avoid much physical discomfort, and high enough to experience all of what I'd consider its primary positives. I wouldn't take a large dose again and I think there are better substances to experiment with at these intensities. 


(That said, the 40mg trip was great fun. It was an accidentally high dose and I was thoroughly miserable for the first 30 minutes of proper effects, then it occurred to me that people take the drug for *fun* and the idea was so ridiculous that I creased up laughing for god knows how long. After I finally stopped laughing I was in a great mood for the rest of the trip. I went to play snooker that morning with residual visuals and was better than usual).

<!-- POST END: id=10360686 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10621827 num=241 author=Ineffable14 author_id=244057 date=2012-05-26T16:30:02+0100 -->
### Post #241

| Field | Value |

| Page | 13 |

**Piracetam+2c-I combo**


Well, its been a while since I had this particular experience, I wanted to share this this info with all of you as I found this combo much more enjoyable that 2c-i alone.


I had been taking the pira for two weeks, 2400mg a day, three doses of 800mg each time. The day I was to drop the 2c-i, I took an attack dose of 2400mg and then, three hours later, took 800mg followed by my 18mg dose of 2c-i.


The trip came on slow, comeup began after about an hour and a half. A few friends and I decided to venture out of the campgrounds and into the music festival we were attending. As we got inside, I began to feel an extreme euphoric energy come over me. I felt like some kind of neon- electric child. (If that make any sense lolz) The visuals I had walking around the festival where some of the most intense and intricate visuals I've ever seen on 2c-i (even at doses up to 23mg), I was seeing the clouds shift and melt at great speeds. The grass took on the form of a living persian carpet, patterns swaying and dancing to the music. I remember looking into a crowd of people and seeing them take turns leaning over and vomiting streams of color, took me like 5 minutes of staring at them to realize they were just hoola-hooping, the vomit i thought I was seeing was the hoola-hoop. I saw a cloud take on the shape of the centipede from the animated movie James and the Giant Peach, he was looking down at the festival, smiling with his tongue out, holding a triton, was weird shit. We walked around and danced for a while before making it to the dance tent for Shpongletron, the stage was a soup of light and color, the music sounding more crisp and clear than on MDMA.


In conclusion, I found that piracetam greatly enhanced the effects of 2c-I. I was shocked as to how visual it was as opposed to it w/o the pira. Also noticed it smoothed out the comedown, I normally feel stimulated well after the effects are over, this post-stimulation was non-existent. I have repeated the experiment with 15mg of 2c-i with similar results.


Hope this is useful information. I personally won't be dosing the iodo again with out some piracetam.

Much love

<!-- POST END: id=10621827 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10721319 num=248 author=WOAHAAHOAH author_id=245030 date=2012-07-05T01:34:28+0100 -->
### Post #248

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10721319 |
| Author | WOAHAAHOAH |
| Author ID | 245030 |
| Date | Jul 5, 2012 at 1:34 AM |
| Page | 13 |

IMO low doses of 2C-I are just not worth it. A lot of people consider the fact that the negative effects of the 2C-I will worsen with higher doses, but that has not been the case IME. I started out doing 25mg every trip, simply because this is the amount that I receive in the capsules I purchase.


25mg is good, and it provides a lucid trip. I've never found 25mg to be intense in the slightest.


However, after I started doubling that dosage and began using 50mg each time, I'm convinced that higher doses of 2C-I are the way to go. When I'm on 50mg of 2C-I compared to 25mg, I'm not thinking about the buzz in my head, my clenching jaw, or the muscle tension. During the peak of the experience, I'm simply CAPTIVATED in visuals. One of the hardest trips I ever had was from 2C-I at 50mg. The watermarking and overlaying of Persian rug patterns, sweeping across the surface of objects, was incredible. I've never had more incredible visuals.


25mg of 2C-I, for me, will cause the walls to look as though an invisible entity is trying to piece together a puzzle of patterns, but is struggling and cannot manage to get a strong structure around these patterns. However, on 50mg of 2C-I, the wall is REDUCED moving patterns that are literally FLOWING with life.


2C-I is not a big CEV'er for me, but at 50mg, the CEV's are breathtaking.


I'd definitely recommend to anyone who feels comfortable with this drug to go for the higher doses. I've only noticed a flip-flop in positive and negative effects and find it to be a much more rewarding experience.

<!-- POST END: id=10721319 -->

### Post #263

theres the 2ci big and dandy aswel. 


2ci is a rewarding chem for me was my first rc, lasts around 6-8 hours for me. has a stimulating edge to it which i find pleasurable. i usually come up fully at around 1 hour marker, this is on a emty stomach. now i have had some batches that took a couple hours to kick in, those batches were also a little weaker than others intensity wise but had a little longer duration, weird. the headspace is also very clear i can function pretty well on 2ci iv had multiple convos with older people while on 2ci and they would have never guessed i was catching visuals at the time lol. it does stimulate thinking to a nice degree as well but nothing overwhelming/pushy for me. visuals are also really nice imo, lots of sparkling, color enhacement, things look eally detailed and sharp/clear imo. i also always see colored splotches all over the walls kinda like graffitti. 


sorry if im no help, good luck with your 2ci have fun and safe tripping.

they are repetitive like with most PEAs i have tried, points and edges on objects get real crisp and clear, for me it made my vision very clear like crystal clear, alot of times id feel like im in a fish bowl or under water. lots of fractals and pixels and pastel like art like paintings, for me visuals will get going pretty nicely there will be patterns all throughout my visual field, some it doesnt effect that way some claim its barely visual to them but for me its pretty visual everyones different. visuals are smooth for me, things flow together nicely. 


this 1 experience(40mg hcl) i got settled into a state that was very euphoric and my eyes were rolling and for like 5 min i was in the labrinth style landscape, i couldnt tell up from down they looked the same, everything looked like mirrors. this was with lots of cannabis aswel. i could also feel myself slipping into this state and i was playing around at first to see if i could pull out if i got scared and i kept poppin in and poppin out then i finally jjust stepped through and thats when i slipped into that state fully. was really nice wasnt pushy at all. i was iffy about it at first because it was when i was first messing with 2cx compounds but it turned out to be very rewarding.

I've always been aware of a South American theme to my visuals on 2C-I - lots of patterns and hieroglyphs that could be from the Aztecs or Mayans.


I also tend to see an awful lot of eyes (wood is particularly amazing - the grain in a door revealed a multitude of inquesitive eyes)


I would agree that overall there seems to be a real sense of clarity in general, less obvious colour hues than some psychedelics - but still fairly beautiful CEVs.

| Page | 14 |

Would suggest not doing the diazepam unless things go sour while tripping, benzos tend to dull down the trip and can leave you just confused . If you need it, drop the pill under your tongue and it will kick in very quickly. Other than that, benzos and PEAs seem to be safe to combine.

<!-- POST END: id=10818519 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10818603 num=270 author=Redbong author_id=208644 date=2012-08-12T14:39:07+0100 -->

| Post ID | 10818603 |

| Page | 14 |

Diazepam should bring you down some. I wouldn't take it first for fear of ruining the experience. Might be good to have on hand, in case the intensity gets too much. 2c-i tends to cause me a lot paranoia. Set and setting are key. 


As far as visuals go, 2c-i has been some of the prettiest. It's like being in a psychedelic river. Everything it flows over bends, shifts, and changes color.

<!-- POST END: id=10818603 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10819416 num=271 author=deficiT author_id=185147 date=2012-08-12T20:41:34+0100 -->
### Post #271

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10819416 |
| Author | deficiT |
| Author ID | 185147 |
| Date | Aug 12, 2012 at 8:41 PM |
| Page | 14 |

On that low dose, you'll probably just get a very pleasant(for me) stimulating body high, and a general mood lift, once you overcome any comeup anxiety. Things will just be more colorful, wavy, and pretty looking. Can be kinda nauseating as the high comes in waves, with one minute you may be feeling kinda sober, and the next you may be tripping. Was the first phenethylamine other than amphetamine I ever tried, and i prefer it because I'm experienced with it and it's a very easygoing trip for the most part. Using benzo's for the comedown is safe.

<!-- POST END: id=10819416 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10861688 num=274 author=biffhenderson author_id=219041 date=2012-08-30T18:36:37+0100 -->
### Post #274

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10861688 |
| Author | biffhenderson |
| Author ID | 219041 |
| Date | Aug 30, 2012 at 6:36 PM |
| Page | 14 |

16mg 2C-I was dissolved in a small amount of warm 80 proof liquor which was mixed into a fruit smoothie.  Comeup was slow and gentle.  I did experience some elevated pulse and a noticeable increase in body temperature, but I'm fit and healthy so no worries.  Starting at about +4:30 I had some GI discomfort but I would rate it as minor.  At about +5:00 I had a slight urge to clench my jaw, but again, minor.  Noticeable central nervous system stimulation.  On three different points during the trip I got up and started vacuuming, just because I decided the floor needed it.  I can assure you that spontaneous vacuuming is not a behavior I have history of.


It was a very good trip.  My mental state was positive the entire time.  Anxiety and worries took the day off.  There is no doubt I got to +++.  If I focused on a object in the room such as a piece of furniture it would start coming towards me.  Patterns covered the walls when I cared to look.  90 degree angles became obtuse.  Mindfuck is such a pejorative term, lets call it "altered concept".  There was almost none.  No confusion.  Best part is my fingers were unimpaired enough to play a musical instrument, which I did for hours fueled by central nervous system stimulation.  Got out a fancy echo machine and played with sound on sound long delays a la Brian May or the Edge.  Fun for hours, it never got old.  


At about +6:00 I smoke a eyeballed amount of 5-MEO-DMT.  It was probably about 10mg as I did not achieve break though and did not leave this mortal coil during the experience.   5-MEO-DMT experiences are impossible to put into words, but I'll try.  After releasing the smoke I heard a sort of tinnitus-like sound and a powerful feeling of positive energy and joy came flowing up through my body starting at the base of my spine - is that the kundalini?  The feeling was ecstasy.  It was joy and love and eternal blessings (odd choice of words from an atheist).  


Sleep came easily at about +9:00.  


The next day I woke up with a new optimism about life.  Sure, I have stuff to worry about and past failings to be feel sorry about.  But it's time to stand up straight and get to work and make the best of what I have.  Instead of complaining, how about seeing how good you can be?  Not lucky in love?  Then get your ass down to the gym and then get some.  I think I've discovered the purpose of life.  It's to work and to love until the day we die.


That was a good trip.

<!-- POST END: id=10861688 -->

<!-- POST START: id=10863472 num=275 author=desertracer543 author_id=234619 date=2012-08-31T07:22:06+0100 -->
### Post #275

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 10863472 |
| Author | desertracer543 |
| Author ID | 234619 |
| Date | Aug 31, 2012 at 7:22 AM |
| Page | 14 |

I just would like to add that this substance is beautiful. I have had the opportunity to research it several times in the past few months, and am very please with it. Unfortunately it's illegal in the states now :/ 15-17 mg was great. My good friend described it as similar to candy flipping (I've never candyflipped before). 20-21mg was even better, I never went past that dosage. I have never taken a psychedelic that makes me laugh as much as 2C-I does. I was laughing "geekin" for upwards to 6 hours, whereas on other drugs there's usually a much shorter period of time where I get the giggles. It has such a positive mindset and beautiful visuals. 20mg was similar to a lower dose of acid for me but there was also increased tactile sensations! Overall I would say that 2C-I was therapeutically for me in several ways...I came out of it with a very positive attitude for life (more so than usual) and feel more connected to those few friends that also tripped with me.

<!-- POST END: id=10863472 -->

my first real attempt with this substance I was missold 2c-i as 2c-b (I was fairly aware though as the 0.5g bag had a big 'i' on it.


took one capsule of 28mg orally, later tailed by around 15mg intranasally.


The experience was a hell of a ride, especially being out at a rave.


At peak the visuals were too strong, I couldn't see a metre in front of me and kept losing my friends faces in my own vision


My feelings and subconscious would be projected into my OEVs 


There was a little bit of paranoia, i.e. thought the cab journey home wasn't actually a real cab but in fact a simulation designed to let people wind down after the rave.


However, I think the experience is fairly malleable despite the strength as I didn't really have any negative thoughts and the setting I was in could have easily induced fear.


How many of you do 2c-i on your own? I have a fear of getting very bored?

<!-- POST START: id=11566874 num=279 author=eithne author_id=253988 date=2013-05-17T08:22:12+0100 -->
### Post #279

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 11566874 |
| Author | eithne |
| Author ID | 253988 |
| Date | May 17, 2013 at 8:22 AM |
| Page | 14 |

Has anyone else ever experienced a 2c-i trip going on past the 6-8 hour mark? The last time I took it I didn't come down for about 16 hours, the majority of which was experiencing the full of what I'd taken. Thankfully we'd dosed normal/threshold dose (My friend dosed us and I didn't know enough about it at the time to remember exactly how much, even though I did ask and he told me.) and I was in a good place so I didn't mind too much. We'd been planning to trip and then go to a friend's birthday when we came down, but while I was perfectly capable of going outside and interacting with people, I didn't really want to. Just to give a time frame, in the entire duration of my trip my friend tripped with me, came down, went to the party, dosed a few other people and himself again and they were coming down again not long after I was able to get to sleep. I stayed at home and just chilled out, enjoyed the visuals, made myself a little nest in the corner of my room with my duvet and just zoned out listening to music until I was finally capable of sleep.


I'd taken 2c-i twice before that, over about a year, and the duration of both trips was about 6 hours and then residual stimulation or whatever, but I'd been prescribed and started taking Lamictal for epilepsy before the most recent trip. My poor friend, I scared the crap out of him because he thought I was having a seizure and I wasn't in quite the right mind to explain how I knew I wasn't because of the differences in what I was feeling ![:P](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f61b.png) Words, man.


I've done some cursory searches, but I haven't been able to find too much about Lamictal's interactions with any psychs at all, let alone the 2c family, so I'm wondering if it was just a fluke, or if my medication is maybe affecting the dose/response curve or my ability to metabolise it. I haven't come across any more 2c-i since the last time to do any more 'experimenting', but I got some 2c-b lately and I really want to try it, but I'm understandably a bit hesitant, especially since the people I would be tripping with are pretty inexperienced.


So, anyone got any experiences or anything they can share?

<!-- POST END: id=11566874 -->

<!-- POST START: id=11572934 num=280 author=LabRatPsychonaut author_id=282040 date=2013-05-19T21:52:22+0100 -->
### Post #280

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 11572934 |
| Author | LabRatPsychonaut |
| Author ID | 282040 |
| Date | May 19, 2013 at 9:52 PM |
| Page | 14 |

Hey eithne, I have been experimenting with 2ci for the past three months now, and have taken only oral doses ranging between 25 - 44 milligrams. I have probably tripped on 2ci between 12 -15 times now, and must say it is an amazing substance. I experience no nausea or body load while on this substance, or intense headaches/depression afterwards like other users of this substance have reported. It takes me between an hour and an hour and forty five minutes to peak on 2ci, and the peak always tends to last me 6-7 hours with doses between 25-35 milligrams. The past few times I tripped, when taking 38, 41, and  just a few days ago 44 milligrams, the peak tends to last 8-10 hours. The most intense of effects, (CEV and OEV's) seem to slowly disappear around the 8 or 9 hour mark, but I definitely notice strong effects for about 12 hours when taking a dose higher than 38 milligrams. I also would like to note that unlike most other people, I do not seem to suffer from any lasting visual effects (HPPD) after taking 2ci. I'm sorry but I am not aware of the interactions of Lamictal and 2ci, I just figured I would add my two cents here as this seems to be my favorite psychedelic. I have done 2ce about 10 times, and I notice that 2ci is much more visual for me ironically. I do not really enjoy the introspective qualities of 2ce as much as I enjoy the effects of 2ci. I can't help but smile the majority of the trip on 2ci, and find myself doing a variety of things from hiking with friends, climbing things, and skateboarding. The most intense visuals I have experienced with it to date were on my most recent trip in my room with the blacklights on, where I didn't just experience the walls/carpet morphing and crawling, but actual shapes and fluorescent colored lines appearing right in front of me. I hope this information is of some use to somebody, I just can't stress all the positive experiences I've had with this chemical.

<!-- POST END: id=11572934 -->

<!-- POST START: id=11573077 num=281 author=zn13bt author_id=160808 date=2013-05-19T23:03:31+0100 -->
### Post #281

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 11573077 |
| Author | zn13bt |
| Author ID | 160808 |
| Date | May 19, 2013 at 11:03 PM |
| Page | 15 |

Lamictal is an anti-seizure medication, while psychedelics can make seizures more likely to occur in people who are susceptible to them. Generally it's not a good idea to mix the two classes of drugs.

<!-- POST END: id=11573077 -->

<!-- POST START: id=11863806 num=282 author=eithne author_id=253988 date=2013-10-03T08:04:28+0100 -->
### Post #282

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 11863806 |
| Author | eithne |
| Author ID | 253988 |
| Date | Oct 3, 2013 at 8:04 AM |
| Page | 15 |

Months after the fact, I return having recently taken 2c-b, and I do think lamictal affects the 2c family. I tripped fairly strongly - but not uncomfortably so, just right I'd say, on the precipice - off 15mg, and stronger and for longer than my friends, who had taken 25mg. I'm pretty much considering it a free bonus at this point, and just another thing to take in account when planning to take psychedelics, but I know that sentiment will hardly be universal. It would be great if there was anyone else on lamictal/lamotrigine who could corroborate my experiences.


Yup, I'm also aware of the risks of taking drugs on my medication/having epilepsy. I started experimenting with drugs before I was diagnosed, so if I hadn't been I probably wouldn't have started, but I enjoy it too much, tbh. I'm very cautious though; I'm aware of my seizure threshold and I can tell how far I can push my health and never have any problem stopping dead if I think it's time. But my main triggers are stress and sleep deprivation. I have yet to have a seizure which was attributable solely to drugs/drinking, it's exclusively been when I was an idiot and pushed myself to stay awake for too long.


For anyone interested, I'm currently prescribed 150mg in the morning and 175mg.


I know it's probably ridiculously stupid, but I feel safe enough to use myself as a bit of a guinea pig for others who may be epileptic/prescribed lamictal and would like to experiment. It's going to happen anyway and there's barely any information out there regarding it. If anyone has any questions, feel free.

<!-- POST END: id=11863806 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12092655 num=283 author=Lococo author_id=291893 date=2014-01-20T16:03:05+0000 -->
### Post #283

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12092655 |
| Author | Lococo |
| Author ID | 291893 |
| Date | Jan 20, 2014 at 4:03 PM |
| Page | 15 |

Recently I was given a sample of 2C-I (I'd say between 12-18mg), I dissolved it in water and drank it on down. I started feeling the come-up around +1:30 with the general head buzz and very mild CEV's. Around +2 I was at a +++, and this was beginnging to feel very much like a mushroom trip. OEV's were present, things were waving and wiggling and distorting (as I usually experience on shrooms), and my brain was beginning to open up and form thoughts that it doesn't normally formulate under normal circumstances. A friend and I made the trip to a small, crowded bar to check out an awesome band, and normally where I'd be a bit perturbed at being canned into a small area like a sardine, this was mostly Phamily and the love I felt coming from everyone was INTENSE. I normally like to think of myself as being somewhat an empath, but tonight it was extra strong. I would see a woman dancing with her boyfriend, and could literally feel the love between the two. I could stare at the scantily clad, seductive temptress in the corner dancing and grinding against the wall, and could feel the sexuality she was putting off. 

To sum everything up, 2C-I was almost identical to a mushroom trip for me, the only part missing was the connection with the Oneness I can usually experience with mushrooms. It had the heavy-headed feeling I get on most 2C's, but it wasn't debilitatingly heavy like 2C-D or 2C-E. All in all, it was an awesome experience and I would definitely have some more experiences with this wonderful substance

<!-- POST END: id=12092655 -->

---

OEV's were present, things were waving and wiggling and distorting (as I usually experience on shrooms), and my brain was beginning to open up and form thoughts that it doesn't normally formulate under normal circumstances. A friend and I made the trip to a small, crowded bar to check out an awesome band, and normally where I'd be a bit perturbed at being canned into a small area like a sardine, this was mostly Phamily and the love I felt coming from everyone was INTENSE. I normally like to think of myself as being somewhat an empath, but tonight it was extra strong. I would see a woman dancing with her boyfriend, and could literally feel the love between the two. I could stare at the scantily clad, seductive temptress in the corner dancing and grinding against the wall, and could feel the sexuality she was putting off. 
> 
> To sum everything up, 2C-I was almost identical to a mushroom trip for me, the only part missing was the connection with the Oneness I can usually experience with mushrooms. It had the heavy-headed feeling I get on most 2C's, but it wasn't debilitatingly heavy like 2C-D or 2C-E. All in all, it was an awesome experience and I would definitely have some more experiences with this wonderful substance
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Lococo said:


Awesome time it sounds like.  Any residue/excess stimulation?  Those properties are what helped me decide to move on from 2C-I but I seem to be in a minority of people.

<!-- POST END: id=12092675 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12150541 num=286 author=Shpongleton author_id=301437 date=2014-02-15T06:28:44+0000 -->
### Post #286

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12150541 |
| Author | Shpongleton |
| Author ID | 301437 |
| Date | Feb 15, 2014 at 6:28 AM |
| Page | 15 |

I tried my first sample of 2C-I a few days ago and felt like sharing a bit of my experience. I weighed out around 10mg, choosing to start at a relatively safe dose for the first time. I am very familiar with 2c-e, 4-ho-mipt, and to a lesser degree dipt. Perhaps it was because I took it on a completely empty stomach, or possibly because it was a new substance that I was unfamiliar with, but I had a fairly strong and all together very worthwhile experience. Within 15 minutes of ingestion I was already at a +++ struggling to deal with the speed it hit me. It should be noted here that 2C-I does not seem to dissolve in water very well especially when it's clumped together. Despite violent swirling the powder refused to separate and dissolve. The taste when it hit my tongue was terrible.


Overall the trip seemed to lack the sort of inner struggle that I am so used to on other psychedelics, even at low doses. I found it easy to let go, driven partially by an emotional core and less of the sort of enigmatic intensity of other psychedelics. There wasn't exactly any sort of deep insight but it felt as if I had no need to try to understand any of it because it all just made sense anyways. On 2c-e I get into deep thought loops and linearity is all distorted while on 2c-i I felt none of that. Deep? Yes. Enigmatic? No. This is not to say I did not get strong hallucinogenic effects because I reached a novel moment where I felt my body disconnect as if my arms and legs and head were no longer attached to the rest of my body. I felt my head rise up and away from my body, detached and floating. Music did not seem to have the striking focus of 2ce instead taking on warped and chaotic forms which lacked strong synaesthetic clarity.  But it was a very helpful trip and not at all like the easy stimulating experience I was expecting. It was as if 2C-I was deceptively easy despite the obvious insanity of the experience, which was exactly what I needed. Definitely a strong and worthwhile phenethylamine, to be treated with respect like any other psychedelic.

<!-- POST END: id=12150541 -->

<!-- POST START: id=12182459 num=301 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2014-03-02T18:44:50+0000 -->
### Post #301

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12182459 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 2, 2014 at 6:44 PM |
| Page | 16 |

I really like 2C-I as well.  I generally don't find it very deep but I have had really surprising moments on it.  The visual effects are very interesting.  Everything appears very fuzzy and warm.  Size distorts.  I seem to have people experience contact highs quite often (which is also mentioned in PiHKAL).  The strangest effect I have had from it reminded me of a trip report on Erowid I have read since.  I noticed once I hit the peak that around the corners of my vision, I could see energy forms all over my apartment, moving around, approaching or moving away from me, or even staying up.  But every time I moved my gaze, two distinct shapes like hands, but as invisible energy fields (I saw them as shimmering outlines like heat shimmers), crossed down from above and covered my vision, like hands were covering my eyes and blocking this new sight.  But I started looking at things out of my peripheral because the hands weren't blocking that, and I noticed an energy field that looked like a 7 year old little bot, who was shyly approaching me, and I told him it was okay and then he moved close to me to hang out, I suppose.  Then in the doorway I saw a stern, middle-aged man, just watching over us.


The next morning I was hanging out with my girlfriend at the time, and she casually asked me if I had ever seen spirits in our apartment.  I asked if she had, and she proceeded to tell me about a 7 year old little boy and a stern-faced middle aged man who seems to just be watching over us and the little boy.  Then a bit later, we told the little boy that he could come hang out with us, and then the cats started watching a spot in the middle of the air and the spot they were looking at got closer and closer, and once it reached the room we were in, we heard thumps on the floor like footsteps and then a *wham* we could actually feel on the floor next to us.  


That experience has stuck with me, it was pretty crazy and I don't know how else to explain it than 2C-I was making me see something real.

<!-- POST END: id=12182459 -->

Hey bluelighters, I have a question!

I have just been put on penicillin for an infection in my toe. I've been planning to drop a capsule of ~25mg of 2c-i this weekend though. I take 660mg phenoxymethylpenicillin 3 times a day. Would there be any adverse reactions between my penicillin and the 2c-i?

<!-- POST START: id=12265718 num=306 author=pharmakos author_id=109521 date=2014-04-10T18:38:18+0100 -->
### Post #306

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12265718 |
| Author | pharmakos |
| Author ID | 109521 |
| Date | Apr 10, 2014 at 6:38 PM |
| Page | 16 |

^ there likely wouldn't be a direct interaction between the penicillin and the 2C-I, but be cautioned that 2C-I does cause lessened blood flow to your extremities (vasoconstriction) which could cause complications with the infection.

<!-- POST END: id=12265718 -->

I would dose every week to every other week until I burned through 250mgs (besides the one time where I dosed 2 days in a row, which like I said caused some issues therefor wasn't repeated), tolerance wasn't an issue however it should be said that I'm a real phen hardhead. 50mgs of 2c-i with no tolerance is a low/med +++, still fully functional. I felt like I would be able to push the dose higher if it wasn't for the stimulation, it was just too much at high doses.

2c-e is a whole 'nother game, I don't push this one as far as I would other 2c's... 25mgs is a solid +++ though I've taken 30mgs twice however that dose was a bit too high IMO. The first time I took 2c-i was 20mgs oral with a 5mg nasal booster (ouch!!!) and that trip was super underwhelming, like a plus 1 1/2. 2c-c is another chem that I really need.to push to get worthwhile effects, 40mgs was threshold however 80mgs was a solid +++, very reminiscent of DOC (especially the cool colored visuals) though many disagree... When it comes to tryptamines though I'm "average", 25mgs of metocin or psilacetin is plenty enough, as is something like 10mgs of oral moxy.

Sorry, I'm too lazy to read through this whole thread.  Just read the last page here.  =)  (Plus it's hard to sift through so many posts looking for specific info.) Sounds like you guys have a Lot of experience.  What's a good starting dose for 2C-I?  I'm only getting a small amount of this so I want to be efficient with it (two 100 mg sacks).  Is there a steep dose response curve?  Good for social settings?  And I'm wondering if this can be combined with 4 ho trypts?  Sorry for the noob questions.

<!-- POST START: id=12616827 num=316 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2014-10-04T17:33:54+0100 -->
### Post #316

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 12616827 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Oct 4, 2014 at 5:33 PM |
| Page | 16 |

2C-I is good starting at maybe 16mg.  The dose-response curve is steep above that.  18mg is a solid trip, and 20mg is strong.  People take it higher than that too, I found 22mg a bit much.  People respond differently but I'd say that's a good guide.  If you try 16 or 18mg and it's not strong enough, go up by 2mg the next time.  


It will mix with 4-HO-trypts I think, I haven't tried that specifically though.  I know 2C-B combines wonderfully with them.  I could imagine 2C-I working too.  I'd try to experience a solid 2C-I trip on its own first though, before you try combining a second psychedelic.


2C-I is a pretty good social drug.  It makes you feel pretty good and happy usually, but it also has a definite psychedelic edge.  I've had uncomfortable moments socially with it but also a lot of really good times.

<!-- POST END: id=12616827 -->

I did 36mg once (had a bunch of 18mg pills, one day decided to take two just to see what would happen, this was years ago when I was inexperienced with everything)

Had a lot of muscle spasms and extreme nystagmus. Also a bizarre vision of being underground in some sort of magickal ceremony, surrounded by entities wearing cloaks over their heads.

Years later I was stunned when I came across a drawing very similar to my vision in a book ([The Underworld Initiation](https://www.amazon.com/The-Underworld-Initiation-journey-transformation/dp/1892137038) by R. J. Stewart).


Anyways, since then I've never gone over 24mg. ![;)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f609.png)

I took this one last night @ 16 mgs.  It was different compared to anything I've done, as the visuals and body high were unexpectedly stimulating and trippy at the same time.  Similar to a candyflip in that way, but different in all other aspects.  The trip seemed very well-rounded since it lasted a good 9 hours or so, wasn't really mind-fucky but the visuals were there, and the comedown was smooth.  The only other 2C I've taken was 2C-P, but it wasn't like that one either.  Xorkoth gave me really good info, since I did feel like my brain was on overdrive from the head high, visuals, mental stimulation and lights had an aura/glow to it.  My visual field seemed uncharacteristically hazy but sharp, especially anywhere too dark or too bright, there were auras there.  It seems like it would be very psychedelic at higher doses.  My mind seemed to race a lot but I never felt uncomfortable.


This 2C-I is a nice chem.  I don't think I'll be combining this with a trypt because it will probably get too trippy.  Taking it on its own feels like a combination of drugs already.

<!-- POST START: id=14247556 num=331 author=Axed author_id=179566 date=2018-01-24T17:28:58+0000 -->
### Post #331

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14247556 |
| Author | Axed |
| Author ID | 179566 |
| Date | Jan 24, 2018 at 5:28 PM |
| Page | 17 |

Sorry to resurrect such an old thread but I want to share my experience ![<3](https://bluelight.org/xf/BL_Images/Orig_Emoji/24.gif) 


I finally got around to trying 2C-I a couple of days ago after having some in my stash for I don't even no how long. I took ~25mg on an empty stomach (I meant to eat beforehand but forgot to - I then tried to down as much of an instant ramen as I could) around 12:30PM and felt it come on around 1PM. I was expecting it to take longer to feel anything, must have been due to my empty stomach. In reading through people's experiences with 2C-I I saw several statements that the bodyload is light and nausea is uncommon. Well I couldn't even eat my whole cup of instant ramen before getting super nauseous and throwing up not once, but twice. This is a bit unusual for me because I do often get nauseous on psychedelics others than LSD, but it usually passes without me vomiting. I also noticed a feeling of electricity or slight tremors in my body. I read on here that a lot of other people experienced that during the comeup so I was not worried at all, nor was it completely unpleasant. 


Anyways, after the second upchuck I finally felt better stomach-wise and the trip really started to unfold. I had strong visuals but not in the patterning or melty variety, more like lots of colors and tracers. I drew a little bit and it was fun to play with colored pencils (usually when I do draw I stick to pen) and let the tracers guide my art. I put some clips of Tipper sets on my tv and they sounded amazing. I mean, I already love Tipper but at some points I was literally snapchatting my friends bits of the sets as if I was actually at a show. The visuals he has for his sets were perfect in the moment as well. 


My mind was relatively clear; I wasn't bogged down with memories that make my feel guilty (like 4-AcO-DMT) or stuck in my thoughts (like 2C-E). One of the things I enjoyed the most throughout the trip was talking to my friends via my phone. A bunch of my friends and I are in a group chat on Snapchat, and two of my friends also decided to trip on the same day in their respective phones. So we were all sending each other ridiculous pictures/videos/etc and I loved the absurdity as well as the sense of connection. Even browsing Facebook was fun, although I only did it for a bit before getting distracted, and I'm not usually one to use my phone much while tripping. 


I spent a good part of the trip watching Dr. Strange for the first time, which was the perfect movie to put on while under the influence of psychedelics. Seriously, if you guys haven't seen it yet, take your trippy drug of choice and watch ASAP. It's basically DMT: The Movie. To the point where it made me deeply consider smoking some deems, but I didn't get around to that. 


I also spent some time playing with my hoop and fire fans, and it felt really good to flow. I felt like I was close to unlocking some new moves but unsurprisingly would get distracted before long and end up doing something else. Food was also delicious once I remembered that it existed. Some psychedelics make me the opposite of hungry for the entire trip, but on 2C-I I could eat after only a couple hours into the trip. I made a very simple tofu meal but it was still super satisfying. 


The trip last around 5 hours, a little shorter than I was expecting. I still felt off from baseline for a few hours after but the visuals and magic were definitely gone. The comedown itself was neutral to unnoticeable and I just felt content from having a very nice day hanging out with myself and my cat. Solo trips are so important and I don't give myself enough opportunities for them. This one was timed just right as I am beginning my second semester of graduate school next week so it was like a way to cleanse my mind before jumping back into that. Overall this was a very pleasant chemical other than the nausea on the comeup. I would take this at a festival but maybe start the trip at the campsite or in an open space in case I need to run to a trashcan/porta potty.

<!-- POST END: id=14247556 -->

Interesting that it was only 5 hours for you, do you tend to metabolize drugs quickly?  It usually lasts 6-8 hours for me.  Anyway, yeah sounds like 2C-I.  I find it to be a fun chemical, pretty euphoric, and pretty clearheaded and sociable.  The exception is that when I take it high enough, my thoughts become very chaotic, not in a profound way, but in a way where I feel somewhat insane.  Difficulty holding a train of thought, lots of weird tangents, nonsense thoughts, etc.

<!-- POST START: id=14677761 num=338 author=Incunabula author_id=174933 date=2019-11-19T03:39:43+0000 -->
### Post #338

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14677761 |
| Author | Incunabula |
| Author ID | 174933 |
| Date | Nov 19, 2019 at 3:39 AM |
| Page | 17 |

2CI was the first RC I tried back in the begining of the 0'ies. It was all the rage in the rave scene in the town I'm from. First I bought a gram with a friend, and when that was gone, I bought one gram just for myself. Dosage wise, 15 mg was a mild trip. 20 mg a strong trip, and over 20 mg I wouldn't take without a tolerance. I did have a freind who spazed out and vomited and lost control on 35 mg. Going over 20 mg it has a steep dose/response curve for sure.


Even before I new what a phenethylamine was, I figured out that it was related to mescaline, even though I hadn't even tried mescaline at that time, just going by the CEV's. Man, they are beautiful. Extremely stylized and mesoamerican indian-like in style. Actually still my favorite CEV's of all psychedelics. 


Now I haven't taken it for ages, even though I still think I have some in the freezer. The downside of 2CI for me, is that it clearly has some heavy noradrenaline/serotonine releasing/inhibition whatever effect. It's much more stimulating than any other phenethylamine I've tried. Leading to teeth clenching aswell as feeling a little down and emotionally worn out the day after. No other 2C's does this for me.

<!-- POST END: id=14677761 -->

> [Incunabula said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=14677761)
> 
> 
> 
> 			Extremely stylized and mesoamerican indian-like in style.
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Incunabula said:


It's funny I always found the visuals to be very much in the mesoamerican style.  2C-I is interesting, I never got much headspace from it but I found it very euphoric and trippy.  It felt superficial, but really fun.  It also gave me some interesting illusions of perspective.  One thing I remember is that at full doses, I would feel like I had a copy of myself, and we shared heads, but my copy extended upwards in t he same position I was in, connected at the head.  As if there was a mirror balancing on top of my head, and everything continued above that mirror.  I could feel the other body as if I existed in both places at once.  It was a really interesting sensation and quite unique.  


Also my first RC. ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)  Well, my first RC I seeked out... my neighbor was selling "foxy" back in 2002, he sold 20mg doses for $20 (we were told 20mg was the dose).  I didn't know anything about it, I only kenw it as some new drug called "foxy".  I enjoyed it quite a bit actually.  But I acquired 2C-I after a lot of research, and it was my first in that sense.

<!-- POST END: id=14677841 -->

<!-- POST START: id=14762778 num=344 author=Buzz Lightbeer author_id=509667 date=2020-03-06T18:21:41+0000 -->
### Post #344

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14762778 |
| Author | Buzz Lightbeer |
| Author ID | 509667 |
| Date | Mar 6, 2020 at 6:21 PM |
| Page | 18 |

10mg plugged was a ++. Comparable to 15-20mg of 2C-B for me (as reference), maybe it didn't absorb all, not sure. Count on 4-5 hours, and then some residual effects that last for a while.


Came up fully in 30 minutes, peak was around two hours. Some visual activity but not like I expected. Some janglyness, but no overstimulation (like a lot of people describe) at all.

It felt really pleasant, the headspace was warm and kind of dreamy at this dose, it's more psychedelic than 2C-B but still similar in that respect. I had a really good time on it, if you can get it, I'd go for it ![:)](https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/joypixels/assets/8.0/png/unicode/64/1f642.png)

<!-- POST END: id=14762778 -->

I'd like to try 2C-I again some time anyways. I didn't realize it was so much more potent that 2C-B, good to note.

<!-- POST START: id=14763116 num=350 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2020-03-06T23:45:11+0000 -->
### Post #350

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14763116 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Mar 6, 2020 at 11:45 PM |
| Page | 18 |

2C-I is cool, I pretty consistently have gotten a somewhat dissociative effect from a full dose.  My most memorable sensation (it happened multiple times) is of there being a mirror of myself attached at the top of our heads, extending up, as if the surface of my head was a mirror, but I could feel my "other self".  It also has really unique visuals and is quite euphoric.  The strongest I've tripped on it was when I preloaded with MXE and ate 12, or maybe 14mg orally.  I descended into crazy visuals and a euphoric and manic head space... I felt sort of psychotic, but in a fun way.  MXE greatly potentiates psychedelics if you use it as a launching pad, normally I would take a good bit more than 12/14mg, more like 20.

<!-- POST END: id=14763116 -->

I always had quite pronounced effects below the 25 mg, think the biggest dose I took was 22 mg, then 18 and had a couple lower ones at 12mg and even one at 2mg which I definitely felt. Ever since that 2mg dose I wanted to try 2c-d because of it purported nootropic effects, I think 2c-i is much more reliable in that aspect, more of push to it, lot more enjoyable too. Very light bodyload, even though I had weird vasoconstrictive issues, or hypersensitivity to it anyways at the higher dosages, bit of a tingle.

Despite being late to the clear net party, thankfully Canada didn’t ban  2cxs (mind 2cb) until like 201something ... and I got to try all these before they disappeared from my radar.

<!-- POST START: id=14784530 num=355 author=Didgital author_id=496462 date=2020-03-30T19:36:30+0100 -->
### Post #355

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 14784530 |
| Author | Didgital |
| Author ID | 496462 |
| Date | Mar 30, 2020 at 7:36 PM |
| Page | 18 |

I've not heard many echo my sentiment that 2c-I is superior to 2c-b when used for aphrodisiac purposes, though I never like to exceed 15mg.


At that dose I find noticable but manageable stimulation, enhanced tactile sensitivity, increased libido, minor visuals, and a certain edge/focus that 2c-b lacks.


In fact, i find 2c-b has a dissociative quality, especially at higher doses. For example, at 24mg i had a full on OBE while in bed with a girlfriend, which was embarrassing quite frankly.


The highest ive taken 2ci was 22mg, and that was a different experience from 15mg. Very psychedelic (particularly CEVs), overstimulating, skin crawly, anxiety.


I still prefer 2cb in general, but not in the bedroom. Granted I've never really explored its use low dose, but I think I prefer a full experience with b for the euphoria and visuals

<!-- POST END: id=14784530 -->

I find 2C-I to be highly visual, and in a totally unique way too that doesn't really resemble other 2C-Xs or any other psychedelic I have tried.  Not as visual as, say, 2C-E, or even 2C-B, but very visual if a large enough dose is taken.  As far as the stimulation, I have had 2C-I trips that felt jittery and weird and some that have felt incredible, euphoric and entactogenic and comfortable.

I’ve taken 2ci, from 2 different batches, years apart, up to 35 mg and while there were visuals, I still wouldn’t describe the entirety of the experience as visual. Jittery and shallow sure lol... hedonistic, perhaps -though I didn’t find it overly pleasurable and haven’t repeated in some years, despite the opportunity. 


Wait, I did try dosing at 17 mg at a hallowe’en party a number of years (5?) ago... and tho it reduced the stimulation to reasonable levels it also reduces the degree of psychedelia - and IMO it still didn’t warrant the tension headache the next day


Even preloading and dosing throughout with magnesium, though helpful, wasn’t enough. 


Mind I seem rather insensitive to 2cs. Perhaps due to expectations, or more likely metabolic factors but either way I don’t seem to get as much from

<!-- POST START: id=15187137 num=368 author=Xorkoth author_id=77889 date=2021-05-21T00:55:48+0100 -->
### Post #368

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15187137 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | May 21, 2021 at 12:55 AM |
| Page | 19 |

Every time I have snorted 2C-Xs (including 2C-I), it felt like I had been kicked in the face, while someone was drilling out my nasal cavity with a power drill.  The pain started pretty quick and grew in intensity and peaked at around 10-15 minutes in.  By then my entire existence was pain, throbbing pain, just absolutely terrible, pacing around, tripping balls, wishing I hadn't snorted it.  After 20 minutes or so it would chill out but it's no way to start a trip.  I have heard other people say it's not so bad but so many people experience something like what I felt.  However it does peak harder and stronger than even plugging.


You could make a nasal spray, as that should greatly reduce the pain, but with only 10mg, it might be hard to actually dose it all.


You can also snort 1-2mg at a time, and alternate nostrils.  That helps.

<!-- POST END: id=15187137 -->

2C-I is speeder, and more euphoric, and the visuals are very unique, not like any other psychedelic.  There is an almost dissociative aspect to the vody high, too.  It is more purely recreational, I never got anything really useful from the mind state but it's fun and unique.  Quite dissimilar from the other 2C-Xs, or anything else.

<!-- POST START: id=15222336 num=383 author=sin_is_synthetic author_id=437130 date=2021-06-22T22:22:16+0100 -->
### Post #383

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15222336 |
| Author | sin_is_synthetic |
| Author ID | 437130 |
| Date | Jun 22, 2021 at 10:22 PM |
| Page | 20 |

It had been 20 or so years since I did 2C-I and I was able to find a source for a very small amount recently that had been properly taken care of. I weighed out about 18 mgs and did not know what to expect.


I love this chemical. It has a little different effects than I remember but this is more due to being a different person than I was and different experiences shaping the journey as it still had an aura that was the same as the one I remembered in 2003.  One thing I got to say- music is absolutely visceral.  Like sometimes so intense that I had to stop and take a deep breath- every note had a tactile response and was paired with a color in my minds eye.  Deep rich blues and purples and neon greens-I always had this experience when phenethylamines have more blues and purples than tryptamines but I don't know if thats for everyone.


I listened to an album by Zakir Hussein and Shivkumar Sharma called The Flow Of Time. Sharma plays a lesser known instrument called a santoor which sonically is somewhere in between a sitar and a xylophone.  Its staccato like a xylophone or piano but it has the effect when played fast that sounds like a metallic ball rolling. I got these visuals of tubes of folding metal stretching off into eternity-contracting like wires to the edge of space. It was  was so real and tactile that I felt I was touching the metal.  There's a lot I sadly didn't remember to write down which will be my focus next trip.


I am looking forward to diving back in after a week or so. All I can say is I wish this was more plentiful as it is a gem.

<!-- POST END: id=15222336 -->

2c-e was the worst bodyload for me. I don't enjoy sweating and repeatedly projectile vomiting. I still managed to work my way through a gram of it though.

<!-- POST START: id=15293863 num=397 author=Kaleida author_id=377522 date=2021-09-07T00:27:27+0100 -->
### Post #397

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15293863 |
| Author | Kaleida |
| Author ID | 377522 |
| Date | Sep 7, 2021 at 12:27 AM |
| Page | 20 |

I would say snort all 2Cs and especially 2C-I at your own risk and not with any regularity if you like your nose. A decade ago I knew someone who was selling 2C-I as a regular street drug convinced that it would be the next LSD, and he would give me massive discounts just because he had no car and would ask me for rides just to do regular daily shit. One time he showed me his supply; he had nearly an ounce of powder. For a brief time period, he and his friends would snort 40-50 mg repeatedly throughout the day, every day, while also going through cases of nitrous oxide. After a couple months of this they stopped when the guy started getting nosebleeds and stuck his finger up his nostril only to feel a massive hole back there. There was also some story about having taken such a high dosage that no more 2C-I would ever be necessary anyway to go along with the decision. These crazy assholes, at one point he told me they gave someone like ~200 mg to snort and told him to take it all at once just to see how he reacted and supposedly he was fine, but refused to say anything about the trip. They were also the kind of friend group to give someone a bowl of 100X salvia and tell them it's a form of hash.


In any case, I really wish I had some more 2C-I. Back then it was the only non-classic psychedelic I had used besides 4-AcO-DMT and in comparison to a newbie's exploration of high dosages of mushrooms, LSD, and DMT, I was relatively unimpressed with the 2C-I, but honestly, a decade and dozens of research chemical psychedelics later, it actually does really stand out. All of the halogenated 2Cs are actually kind of amazing and near perfect drugs even though people tend to think of them as being on the lighter side, and they do go beyond their reputation. 2C-I has still actually given me some of the strongest visionary imagery of things like swimming or tessellated reptiles and the kind of imagery that presumably inspired Native American architecture when it occured on mescaline compared to all the other psychedelics I've taken so far, and tends to do so in a relatively gentle way, and that's not the only good part about it, but it's something I really like.


Should have made more of an effort to make a lasting supply back then. Ah well.

<!-- POST END: id=15293863 -->

|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15293893 |
| Author | Xorkoth |
| Author ID | 77889 |
| Date | Sep 7, 2021 at 1:00 AM |
| Page | 20 |

Yeah the visuals of 2C-I are very unique, I would reliably get this effect where letters (on screen, my keyboard, in a book, etc) would appear like hieroglyphs, but I could still read them.   I would get very mesoamerican stylistic visuals, very strong visuals, it also had a dissociative element to it where my body would feel displaced.  I would frequently get a feeling/sensation where a mirror image copy of myself was attached to the top of my head by the top of its head, and the copy would extend above me, upside down like my head was pressed against a mirror, and I could feel both bodies.  I also had a really crazy experience one time of seeing spirits in my peripheral visual, I had some interactions with two of them and the next morning I mentioned to my girlfriend at the time that I had encountered some spirits last night, and she was like oh is it the little boy and the older man?  I've seen them too.  And she described them exactly like I had experienced them.  Then the cats started reacting as if something was coming towards us and we said hey, if you're the little boy, you can come sit with us (because he seemed shy).  And then right after that there was a thump that we heard and felt that sounded like someone sitting down in front of us (I was no longer tripping and she never tripped once in her life).

<!-- POST END: id=15293893 -->

---

<!-- POST START: id=15293904 num=399 author=Kaleida author_id=377522 date=2021-09-07T01:34:12+0100 -->
### Post #399

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15293904 |
| Author | Kaleida |
| Author ID | 377522 |
| Date | Sep 7, 2021 at 1:34 AM |
| Page | 20 |

There really isn't anything quite like it, and I looked. I get the dissociated aspect too, and it often made me feel like I was on some kind of alien spaceship made with ancient technology but modern technicolor. The color combinations had some resemblance to 2C-B and 2C-C but not as much as they do to each other, and there was a lot going on with 2C-I that still hasn't been present in those for me. The flowery geometry in particular still really stands out in my memory. It was also good for bizarre synesthesia, like one time I saw the right and left sides of the room growing big and small opposite to one another back and forth while also hearing the right and left side of my hearing the music go loud and quiet in tandem, which was really strange to experience. Actually, the only thing I can recall being similar to that was one time on a blotter I was never able to identify, but had reason to suspect it might be DOI; I need to get around to taking that little bit of that I have....


The experiences you describe sound a lot like a type of dissociation I've become much more acquainted with as of late. I like to think of it as the reason that people like to incorporate ideas of backwards/upside down/mirror worlds in fiction.... One way I've been thinking about it is like a Möbius strip: the strip has only a single surface yet the way it's folded makes it so that you're always relatively on one side or the other at any given point, and if you consider the strip a flatland, then if you travel around the strip one time, you'll end up in the same place, but as your mirror image. Furthermore, if when you begin you already have a duplicate mirror image self, they'll end up where you started. The thing about everything being mirrored is, it may seem extremely different to what you're used to, but it has exactly as much structure as the version of it you're used to; for example, if I flip the valuation claims in the statement "This food is delicious and I love it; I would recommend everyone try it!" it becomes "This food is disgusting and I hate it; I would caution everyone avoid it!" Both are rational sentences, even though they describe completely opposite contexts. This is a concept I had to grasp recently to bring myself back from the edge of insanity, as it's impossible to trust anything when you perceive reality in two opposite ways that seem equally stable, and both supported by the things everyone says to you, even if it's that one version is telling you you're crazy while the other version is telling you you're sane.


What would life be like if we always perceived things from the other side instead? Would we still agree upon everything? It feels like it sometimes.

<!-- POST END: id=15293904 -->

Having done it this way so long, I feel like proper labels would only be more incriminating. Terrible scientist of me though! At work we have barcoded labels, printer labels, etc. when I can get away with it, I still just write on it quick with a sharpie.


Harm reduction and jokes aside: label your chemicals. It would be very easy to confuse 2ce for 2cb for example and just have a really bad time due to dosing higher than expected. Or even worse with different chems if you happen to have DOx around.  My repertoire is limited to a handful of substances that are labeled in short hand or otherwise obvious to the sole user


> [izo said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=15295629)
> 
> 
> 
> 			i had 2c-i multiple times, i didnt like it very much, the iodine is too heavy, 2c-b was a lot better.
>

> — izo said:

I wonder if you ever had 2c-c or 2c-d, as they are even lighter still. And I would wager that you haven’t tried..scratch that, that no one at blue light has tried - a **bold statement **- 2C-At with the next heaviest halogen after iodine, Astatine “the rarest naturally occurring element in the Earth's crust, occurring only as the decay product of various heavier elements. All of astatine's isotopes are short-lived; the most stable is astatine-210, with a half-life of 8.1 hours” “the longest lived natural isotope is half decayed in less than a minute” “A sample of the pure element has never been assembled, because any macroscopic specimen would be immediately vaporized by the heat of its own radioactivity.” Only about a gram exists at any given time in all of the earth’s crust and only about 50 micrograms have ever been made at one time!

Of course Shulgin thought of this! I didn’t realize I had already read about this in the extensions and commentary for 2ci!

I moved overseas for seven years, and the friend that was babysitting my chemicals determined that they were her property after all that time. I agreed and bought her a scale. 


I wasn't particularly interested in 2C-I at the time, but it was available. I didn't like stimulants and was looking for insight, and 2C-I didn't sound like it met those criteria. I also tried my first 2C-x (2C-C) before I left the country, and found that it made me feel sickly, which turned me off further. In a 4 hour interview with Hamilton Morris, David Nichols claimed to be the first one to make 2ci.  He doesn't mention a year.

This was pretty surprising to me - I have always assumed it was Shulgin's creation. 


I also learned from that interview that Shulgin created (and patented for use as an antidepressant) methylone.

I think a lot of people attribute a lot of things to Alexander Shulgin that he didn’t do. Several of the drugs he created were actually first synthesized by friends of his who were also chemists, and more of the ideas for drugs he had than people think were really just continuing things other chemists already started, like Albert Hofmann and the synthetic tryptamines.


I think MDMA is the biggest offender. A lot of people don’t seem to realize that MDMA existed before Alexander Shulgin was even born and that it was already in recreational use before he ever even tried it.


> [Xorkoth said:](https://www.bluelight.org/community/goto/post?id=15750946)
> 
> 
>

But I can't imagine it being good for that purpose, except as a rapid acting emergency antidepressant.  maybe if you took really low doses?
> 		
> Click to expand...
> — Xorkoth said:


Back then serotonin releasing agents were new and the idea of taking them for depression didn’t seem so crazy, especially when the main pharmaceutical option for depression was still serotonin reuptake inhibitors and they didn’t really have any stigma yet.


In reality, SRAs are most likely horrible as antidepressants as envisioned back then. They do make good therapy drugs, though.

<!-- POST START: id=15751042 num=419 author=pharmakos author_id=109521 date=2023-02-05T18:36:31+0000 -->
### Post #419

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15751042 |
| Author | pharmakos |
| Author ID | 109521 |
| Date | Feb 5, 2023 at 6:36 PM |
| Page | 21 |

From what I understand, Shulgin named most of the simple 2C-X series, prior to their synthesis.  I never knew that others in the research group handled some of the synthesises tho.  Makes sense that Nichols would have wanted to leave his name out of it at the time tho, he was far more interested in having a career working "inside the lines" so to speak, sticking to academia and working towards having a legitimate academic lab with a DEA license.  I'm sure he got up to ALL kinds of crazy shit that he just managed to hide well lol.


Nichols was my hero more than Shulgin after awhile, back when I was more serious about wanting to pursue neurochemistry.  Going to work at his lab at Purdue was my pipe dream.


Total off topic aside here, but Myron Stolaroff is another wonderful writer from the Shulgin research group, if anyone is interested in the other members.  He wrote a few good works on psychedlics and spirituality, most famously The Secret Chief Revealed, the biography of Leo Zeff. Zeff was the psychologist that Shulgin passed MDMA to for underground use in therapy back in the day, the godfather of MDMA assisted psychotherapy.


Heck I think that book is on the MAPS site for free now that I think about it!


Edit -- here, tracked down the link [https://maps.org/images/pdf/scr.pdf](https://maps.org/images/pdf/scr.pdf)


And here is Stolaroff's work From Thanatos to Eros, which has discussion on many different  psychedelics, mostly 2C-X and MDX from what I recall (been a long time since I read it)


##### Thanatos To Eros, 35 Years of Psychedelic Exploration – Multidisciplinary Association for Psychedelic Studies – MAPS


![maps.org](https://www.bluelight.org/community/proxy.php?image=https%3A%2F%2Fi0.wp.com%2Fmaps.org%2Fwp-content%2Fuploads%2F2021%2F11%2Fcropped-MAPS-logo-handsweb.png%3Ffit%3D32%252C32%26ssl%3D1&hash=126d422098c88daf67edfb5a864fe4f0&return_error=1)

					maps.org

porkstock 2ce was my first RC too, along with 4-aco-DMT and I also loved it for quite a while being second real psychedelic I tried after LSD (not counting morning glory seeds) and wouldn't mind revisiting intense and unique visuals again, though not as much as I would like 4-aco-DMT as I didn’t explore it nearly as much as 2ce. Still those were almost 2 perfect RC’s to start with, at least available at that time.


Concerning 2c’s I tried in years to come, 2c-b is my favourite I also tried 2c-i, 2c-c and 2c-t-4, all unique but if I could chose to get some of those again I would rather explore 2c-c and 2c-t-4 some more than 2c-i, and would definitely revisit 2c-e again rather than 2c-i. The one I really regret not trying is 2c-t-7 and maybe famous 2c-d and 2c-c combo. But hey that’s my preference for relaxing 2c-c compared to more stimulating 2c-i, also 2c-i produced more body load for me compared to 2c-e while still not reaching nowhere near that strong visuals or euphoria and playfulness od 2c-b.

If I add 20mg of 2C-B to that, I will be tripping so hard at the peak that I can't even talk... so many visuals I can't tell what I'm seeing... synesthesia sometimes, followed by a long plateau stage of profound thought and conversation.

I appreciate the response, SpiralusSancti.


I recall now that the main thing that turned me away from 2ci was the adjective "stimulating." I think I have a prejudice against the word, don't like to think of myself doing stimulants I guess? But I do enjoy hiking and being otherwise active during a trip, so maybe it's something I would enjoy. 


I've only tried 2cb as far as other 2cx

They both tend to give me a headache after the trip, and 2ce a bit of sickly feeling during the comeup. 2cp is another one that's an option, but I've never got around to trying. 

I'd probably go for 2cd if I had the option to try any 2cx that's new to me. The 2cT series is intriguing but I think I'd have to steer clear since they don't seem quite as safe

<!-- POST START: id=15751431 num=433 author=Pfafffed author_id=369391 date=2023-02-06T02:45:40+0000 -->
### Post #433

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Post ID | 15751431 |
| Author | Pfafffed |
| Author ID | 369391 |
| Date | Feb 6, 2023 at 2:45 AM |
| Page | 22 |

2C-D gives me a mild next day headache and 2C-C makes me feel weirdly sick (which sucks, because I rather liked it.) I associate regular 2C-B use with an increase in heart flutters for a couple months, but that's very possibly just a coincidence.


I think only the thios (2C-T-7, 2C-T-21) and alkyls (2C-E, 2C-P) have killed people. I don't think any of the halogenated 2C-Xs have. The worst I remember was 2C-I causing HPPD more frequently than other psychedelics, which in the age of NBOx seems almost quaint. All in all, they're remarkably safe.

<!-- POST END: id=15751431 -->
